Important News

Japanese Troops Invading Without Restraint 67

Longjing Village and other places in Jilin have been successively occupied.

Situation in Harbin is tense, rumors of Japanese troops about to invade.

Harbin Dispatch: After the Japanese troops occupied Liaoning and Jilin, they divided their forces into various directions and successively reoccupied Jilin, Liaoyuan, Taonan, Fushun, Andong, Changtu, Sipingjie and other places in our country. On the 23rd, Commander-in-Chief of the Kwantung Army, Shigeru Honjo, ordered the various armies to concentrate their forces in Gongzhuling, with the intention of expanding their military power to northern Manchuria. This, coupled with the Soviet Union's troop deployment in Manchuria, creates a state of high tension with swords drawn. If the Japanese troops advance north, Harbin may become a war zone. I will now relay what I have heard in recent days.

Appointment of Shenyang Mayor: Kwantung Army Commander Shigeru Honjo, after invading and occupying Shenyang, appointed the mayor of Fengtian in the name of the commander-in-chief. The order is excerpted as follows: (1) The Japanese military commander, in view of the current situation near Liaoning City and to promote the happiness of Chinese and Japanese officials and civilians, will implement temporary municipal administration in the area under the guidance of the Kwantung Army Commander from September 20th, Showa 6th year [1931]. (2) The municipal area of Liaoning City will be within the city of Liaoning and the commercial port, with the exception of the Manchurian Railway Affiliated Area, which will continue to be handled according to the previous regulations. The scope of municipal business is specifically defined, including everything related to Liaoning City. (3) The important municipal officials are as follows: Mayor: Colonel of the Army, Kenji Doihara; Chief Secretary: Shunichi Tomiharu; Chief of the General Affairs Section: Shin Ioriya; Chief of the Police Affairs Section: Nagataro Tsuruoka; Chief of the Finance Section: Suetsugu Mitani; Chief of the Hygiene Section: Fukumatsu Morita; Chief of the Engineering Section and concurrently Chief of the Technology Section: Yasushi Kichikawa. (4) Other detailed items will be instructed separately. After Honjo issued the above proclamation, he sent Major General Ninomiya, the commander of the military police, to visit Zang Shiyi and others who were under house arrest, ordering them to place the security regiment under the jurisdiction of the county magistrate under the mayor's administration. Zang replied that the implementation of the municipal system was acceptable, but he hoped that Japan would use the Chinese side's security agency for security purposes and not summon a separate group of police to be under the mayor's jurisdiction. Ninomiya was displeased with Zang's response and left. The Japanese originally planned to implement the municipal system on the 24th, and to hold office at the Shenyang Municipal Office. At the same time, the Fengtian Military and Political Department was established (some say Military and Political Office), with Honjo Shigeru as the head, taking all the military and civilian power of Liaoning into his hands. Later, due to the unfavorable international atmosphere since the 22nd, there was talk of postponing the municipal and military systems.

Disturbances in Shenyang: When Shenyang was suddenly invaded by the Japanese troops, news here was cut off and the truth was unclear. It was once rumored that Zang Shiyi and Rong Zhen were killed. According to those who escaped from Shenyang, Rong Zhen, Wang Yizhe and Huang Xiansheng received news in advance and fled to Xinmin, and the troops were also transferred to the Xinmin Faku area. Zang Shiyi did not have time to escape and was detained by the Japanese troops. Zhang Jinghui, the chief of the special administrative region, was also under house arrest. At present, people inside and outside Shenyang City are panicked, and all shops are closed. There is a severe shortage of food. The poor, unable to obtain food, gathered in front of the grain shops and made a commotion. The Japanese troops actually used machine guns to sweep the crowd, causing numerous deaths and injuries. The Japanese troops also stationed many posts along the streets, searching pedestrians. The Japanese troops would shoot anyone who spoke to each other on the road. Li Yi, the magistrate of Shenyang County, requested the Japanese side to allow the establishment of a self-defense regiment, recruiting 600 police officers to maintain law and order. With the permission of the Japanese side, it was established on the 22nd. However, the Japanese side did not allow them to carry weapons, but only ordered each person to wear a wooden stick and stand on the street to maintain order. The Japanese troops currently stationed in Shenyang City consist of two regiments. The rest have headed north. The two regiments are stationed in the city and outside the city: (1) A part of the 16th Regiment is stationed at the Dongda Camp Arsenal, (2) The 29th Regiment is stationed in the city, (3) A part of the 16th Regiment is stationed in the commercial port area, (4) The 29th Regiment is stationed in the Manchurian Railway Affiliated Area. There are also 80 military police officers, distributed to (1) the East City Detachment, commanded by Captain Matsuura, with the team headquarters set up in the former Palace Telegraph Administration Office, responsible for the security of the city, (2) the City Detachment, commanded by Captain Yamamoto, with the team headquarters set up in the detective office outside Xiaoxibianmen, responsible for the security of the commercial port area, (3) Shanya, the chief of the Fengtian military police detachment, commanded 600 Chinese self-defense police, guarding various parts of the city. After the arsenal was occupied, the usable internal machinery was transported elsewhere by the Japanese troops, and the heavy machinery was blown up. Of the 60 aircraft in the Aviation Department, 20 were newly purchased from the United States and the price had not yet been paid. The Japanese troops wanted to transport them away, but the US consulate knew about it and sent personnel to insert flags and guard them, preventing them from being moved. For the remaining 40 aircraft, the Japanese troops inspected those that were usable and painted the Rising Sun emblem on them, flying around the city and outside the city as a demonstration. The experimental workshop of the College of Science of Northeastern University was bombed by the Japanese soldiers, and personnel were sent to the school to instruct them to hold classes, with all expenses borne by them. However, the students were extremely angry and had all fled.

Course of the Occupation of Jilin: The 19th and 20th Divisions of the Japanese troops stationed in Korea mobilized from Pyongyang on the 19th. When the advance unit, the 77th Regiment, passed through Andong, it occupied Andong. On the 20th, it passed through Fushun and reoccupied Fushun. Half of a battalion of the local army was disarmed, and the rest retreated elsewhere. Benxihu was also occupied. All the larger cities along the Anfeng Line were occupied. After the 19th Division entered Liaoning, the 2nd Division moved north. Division Commander Tamon arrived in Changchun early on the 22nd, and the division headquarters was moved there. At 7:00 that morning, two trains of soldiers, led by Brigadier General Taniya, carrying two infantry regiments and one artillery regiment, advanced along the Jichang Road. At 6:00 p.m., they arrived at Jilin Station. When the merchants in the city heard that the Japanese troops had arrived, they were all panicked and closed their doors. At the same time, a Japanese plane circled in the sky and dropped a bomb at Jilin Station, destroying the ticket office. The explosion was very loud, and people were even more frightened. Many people fled to the countryside. At 7:30 p.m., the Japanese troops entered the city and confiscated the police's firearms, ordering them to maintain order on the ground with their bare hands. Taniya's brigade headquarters was also set up in the Deputy Commander's Office of the Border Defense. Since yesterday, news from Jilin has been cut off, and the situation is unknown. On the evening of the 21st, a division of Japanese troops occupied Longjing Village, Hunchun, Helong, Wangqing, and other areas. Jixing Brigade had retreated to Dongning. The Japanese troops used airplanes to bomb the Juzi Street in Longjing Village, causing great destruction. A part of the army had advanced toward Jilin along the Tiantu Road. Several thousand Koreans transported railway materials, stopping at Huining, and actively built the Jihui Railway under the cover of the Japanese troops. It was heard that Changtu, Taonan, and Liaoyuan had also been occupied by the Japanese troops one after another on the 22nd. The Sidao Road was temporarily managed by more than 100 personnel sent by the Manchurian Railway. Fearing that the Japanese troops would advance along the Taoang Road, which was connected to the Sidao Road, a section of the track was dismantled to prevent them from advancing. Today, it was heard that the Japanese troops are gradually concentrating in Changchun. Judging by their appearance, they may occupy Harbin within a day or two.

Harbin is in extreme danger. The Japanese troops' occupation of Changchun has caused great shock in Harbin. Today (the 23rd), a Japanese plane came to Yaomen on the Hachang Line and circled for a long time before leaving. Yaomen is only 300 *li* from Harbin and can be reached in four hours by express train, so people are even more panicked. The rumors were most rampant last night, with some saying that the Japanese troops would enter the streets soon. At the same time, bombs were said to have been found at the Japanese Consulate, the Korean Bank, the residence of the chief of the intelligence agency, and the Harbin *Nichinichi Shimbun*. The main gate stone of the Korean Bank was damaged, and several frames of type were destroyed at the Harbin *Nichinichi Shimbun*. The glass of the consulate and the residence of the chief of the intelligence agency were shattered, but the explosion was indeed very loud and heard throughout the city, so everyone was in a state of unease. The military and police authorities imposed martial law after 10:00 p.m., and all the police were armed and dispatched. This morning passed peacefully, and people were slightly relieved. However, today the Japanese troops are concentrating in Gongzhuling, and there is talk of heading north. At the same time, the Kason Mixed Brigade of the Japanese troops stationed in Korea has advanced to Liaoning, and the 19th Division has moved to Changchun, so it is rumored that the Japanese troops will arrive in Harbin within a day or two. Tonight, 300 Japanese men and women in Harbin were sent back to their country by the Japanese Consulate. Another group will return to their country tomorrow. Those who have not left are armed and live in the Zhengjin Bank and the police branch office on Maibai Street. Electric nets were set up and sandbags were piled up inside the South Manchurian Electric Company, and the precautions were as if facing a great enemy. (Evening of the 23rd)

A Hunanese

Unanimous Anti-Japanese National Salvation 68

Changsha Dispatch: The people of Hunan Province are extremely indignant at the Japanese troops' trampling on the three northeastern provinces. In addition to organizing propaganda teams to give lectures and strictly implement economic severance, all sectors observed a moment of silence at noon on the 23rd. Today (the 25th) morning, a "Hunan People's Demonstration against the Japanese Military Occupation of Liaoning" was held on the grounds of the Provincial Education Association. All shops in the city were closed, factories were shut down, and schools were suspended. Everyone gathered in teams at 10:00 a.m., with more than 200 groups and about 100,000 people. First, Chairman Hu Yiru reported on the meaning of the meeting and the course of the Japanese troops' atrocities. He said that the number of people attending the meeting today is large and the order is solemn, which is unprecedented. From this, it can be seen that the hearts of the people of the country have not yet died. From now on, we should unanimously eliminate private opinions, concentrate our strength, and prepare everything to fight to the death with Japanese imperialism. In addition, more than ten people including Lei Zhuo Huan, Kang Yi, Ruan Zilin, Zhou Naiji, Zhou Tianpu, and Wei Zhenbang gave speeches one after another. They were all filled with indignation, and the atmosphere was extremely tragic. Then, the presidium proposed ten motions, which were read out one by one on the spot and passed unanimously. At the same time, it was moved to cancel the Hunan Aid Overseas Chinese Association and change it to the Hunan People's Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association. The passed motions were prepared in memorials, and representatives were sent to request the Party and government organs to accept them. Miu Kunshan and Chen Jieshi were immediately appointed to go to the Provincial Government, Wei Zhenbang and Zhou Naiji to the Fourth Route General Headquarters, and Zhou Tianpu and Tang Gan to the Provincial Party Headquarters to negotiate. Then, shouting slogans, they set off on a parade in the order of signing in. Because there were too many people, the route was changed. Starting from East Street of the Education Association, passing through Shuifengjing, turning onto Zhongshan Road, going straight down Fuxing Street, Xichang Street, Taiping Street, Fusheng Street, Pozi Street, Lubianjing, Lijiapo, Xueyuan Street, Nanzheng Street, Hongpailou, Bajiaoting, Zoumalou, Fuzheng Street, Laozhaobi, and Youyicun, returning to the Education Association Ping. It was already after 2:00 p.m. when the meeting was adjourned. The petition to the Provincial Government and the Provincial Party Headquarters is recorded as follows: "Japanese imperialists are taking advantage of our country's troubles to forcibly occupy Liaoning, advance into Tianjin and Shandong, and have the intention of driving straight in. Their secret plans and conspiracies did not originate overnight, and our indecision and misgovernment have caused trouble in peacetime. What our people are most confused about is that the nest is in danger, but the beans are still fried. Disaster is imminent, and who still has lungs and liver? There is no greater hatred than national demise, and no greater sorrow than the death of the heart. Today, what grudges cannot be resolved, what political views cannot be sacrificed? In the face of foreign aggression, private grievances should be released. We should work together in difficult times and share weal and woe. We are frightened by the collapse of China and worried about the safety of the country. The rise and fall of the world is the responsibility of every citizen. The people are indignant and the popular sentiment is boiling. Therefore, at 9:00 a.m. on the 25th of this month, the Hunan People's Demonstration against the Japanese Military Occupation of Liaoning was held on the grounds of the Provincial Education Association. 200,000 people attended the meeting. After deliberation by the whole body, 1. Send a telegram to all countries in the world and the International League to expose the Japanese conspiracy and announce the Japanese atrocities. 2. Send a telegram to the Central Government to issue a clear order to implement conscription. 3. Send a telegram to the Central Government to actively prepare for war against Japan. 4. Send a telegram to Committee Member Hu Zhantang to cancel his leave and jointly maintain national affairs. 5. Send a telegram to all generals in the country to unanimously support Commander-in-Chief Chiang to unify the military and unanimously oppose foreign countries. 6. Send a telegram to persuade Guangdong to break down prejudices, support the Central Government, and unanimously oppose foreign countries. 7. Send a telegram to the whole country to strictly implement economic severance with Japan. 8. Send a telegram to all agencies, shops and factories in the country to not employ Japanese people. 9. Organize a national salvation volunteer army as the government's backing. 10. Send a telegram to all Chinese people serving in Japanese public and private places in the country to automatically withdraw within 24 hours.

The case has been publicly decided and should be implemented unanimously. This association vows to lead the 30 million people of Changsha, Hunan, in photographing the anti-Japanese conference.

With the will to fight against the enemy together and the spirit of saving the country with iron and blood, we will fight bravely, the doctrine will prevail, be the government's backing, be the people's vanguard, and in addition to submitting separately, we should prepare a document stating the facts and submit it to your government for review and assistance, and earnestly ask for separate transfer to the Central Government and order it to be implemented throughout the country, and it is to the point of being unable to wait to be instructed. (The 25th)

Ten thousands citizens of Jiangxi

Anti-Japanese National Salvation Conference 69

Unanimously resolved to send a telegram requesting a declaration of war against Japan

And telegram to Guangdong to end the dispute and jointly relieve the national crisis

Nanchang Dispatch: Since Japan relied on its strength to occupy Liaoning and Jilin, the people of Jiangxi Province have been very indignant, and the anti-Japanese national salvation atmosphere has become tense. Students from schools such as Zhicheng have organized national salvation volunteer armies, posting large slogans of "Pray to die in battle and not be a slave to a subjugated country." All the students from schools such as No. 1 Middle School wear black gauze with the inscription "Engrave it in your heart and swear to save the country" to show their determination to taste bitterness. The business community has also automatically eliminated Japanese goods to economically strangle Japan. The number of military requests to attack Japan is increasing daily. Generals such as Luo Lin sent another telegram to the Central Government yesterday, requesting a prompt order for mobilization to avenge the dead compatriots in Northeast China. According to military sources, provinces such as Hunan, Hubei, Jiangxi, Fujian, Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Anhui, Henan, Gansu, and Shaanxi will soon issue a joint telegram of anti-Japanese national salvation and volunteering to serve. The anti-Japanese national salvation demonstration of the citizens of this city was held on the morning of the 26th at the public sports field. On that day, in addition to flying flags at half-mast throughout the city, all sectors closed down for one day. Therefore, starting from 7:00 a.m., schools, business groups, and Party headquarters at all levels were holding flags and forming teams, carrying small flags to participate. The crowd was as vast as the sea, like a tidal wave. The lecture teams of the schools were also dispatched in full force. The automobile propaganda team drove around the roads, distributing propaganda materials. Aircraft Nos. 107 and 205 dispatched by the Aviation Department soared into the sky, and the leaflets scattered like heavy snow. The entire city was also extremely excited. At 10:00 a.m., various mass organizations arrived one after another, standing in the hot sun in their designated locations, with no less than 100,000 people. Liu Zuozhou of the Provincial Party Headquarters, Jia Guoen of the Municipal Party Headquarters, Wang Jingxin of the Anti-Japanese Association, Zeng Jialin of the business community, Huang Yuncen of the labor community, Liao Zongyu of the student community, and Luo Junqiang of the General Headquarters were elected as the presidium, with Liu Zuozhou as the chairman. After the meeting, the entire body observed three minutes of silence for the compatriots who were killed in Northeast China. Liu reported on the purpose of the meeting, saying that today is the city's entire citizens' tragic and indignant anti-Japanese national salvation conference, because Japanese imperialists never knew what humanity and justice were, and only knew how to seize by violence. They cut off our Ryukyu Islands, took our Taiwan, annexed our Korea, and then forced us to recognize the Twenty-One Demands. Recently, they massacred our overseas Chinese in Korea, still thinking it was not enough, and sent troops into the three northeastern provinces for no reason, determined to destroy China with its thousands of years of history. Now, the Japanese soldiers are tyrannical, and disaster is imminent, so today we are holding this conference to rise up and seek survival together to save the country, and so on. Next, Wang Jingxin of the Anti-Japanese Association, Zeng Jialin of the business community, and Jiang Xiesheng of the Boy Scouts gave speeches one after another. All of them wept bitterly, and the listeners had the feeling of "I will die with you." After the speeches, seven motions were discussed and passed one by one: (1) Send a telegram of condolence to the compatriots who were killed in Northeast China. (2) Send a telegram to the International League to announce the Japanese atrocities. (3) Send a telegram to the Guangdong authorities to support the Central Government and unanimously attack Japan. (4) Send a telegram to the whole country to support Commander-in-Chief Chiang, unify military power, and implement a declaration of war against Japan. (5) Send a telegram to Mr. Hu Hanmin to cancel his leave and take charge of affairs together to relieve the national crisis, and send a telegram to the whole country to urge him to do so. (6) Send a telegram to the Central Government to withdraw the punishment of Foreign Minister Wang Zhengting. (7) Send a telegram to the Japanese proletarian parties, uphold justice, and unanimously oppose their government's aggression and atrocities to maintain peace in East Asia. All of the above cases have been resolved and handed over to the conference secretariat for handling. After the cases were passed, the teams were formed to set off on a parade. The first guide was military music, followed by boy scouts from various elementary schools, followed by students and various industry groups, followed by Party headquarters at all levels, and the rear was guarded by military police. The 100,000 marchers were several *li* long, all marching in neat steps and orderly manner, passing through Huanhu, Zhongshan, and Desheng roads, and shouted slogans along the way in unison, "Down with Japanese imperialism," "Demand that the government declare war against Japan," "Implement economic severance with Japan." The sound shook the roofs, and it did not disperse until about 2:00 p.m. (The 26th)

Another Tragedy on the Beining Railway 70

Japanese Troops Seize Guns from Escort Guards and Railway Police

Major Train Robbery Occurs West of Rao Yang River

Tianjin Communication: Yesterday, another tragedy unfolded on the Guanwai section of the Beining Railway, surpassing the severity of those in recent days. At approximately 12:35 PM yesterday, the Beining Railway passenger train No. 102, heading west from the Huanggu Tun station, was suddenly attacked by a group of bandits along the track west of the Rao Yang River. The bandits opened fire on the locomotive, seemingly aiming to injure the driver. The driver accelerated to full speed, but near the 24th signal cabin, the track had been dismantled for five sections, causing the train to derail. The water tender overturned, the baggage car lay north of the track, and the locomotive and dining car fell south of the track. The first and second-class cars that derailed collided and arched upwards, suffering the most damage. The third-class cars completely derailed and landed on the sleepers. The locomotive had two drivers and three firemen; one driver was injured, and the other four were missing, possibly crushed under the water tender. Due to the wreckage, it was impossible to investigate. A British Indian man in the second-class car was killed in the collision. In the guard's car, the father of a certain railway employee was shot dead by the bandits. Refugees from Shenyang have been fleeing for days, so there were few passengers on the train this time. All of them were transported to Dahu Shan by a train sent by the Beining Railway. Among the first-class passengers were two Italian men and two Dutch men and women, one German woman, and one British Indian man; the deceased in the second-class car was the brother of the British Indian passenger in first class. After the incident, these six foreigners were intercepted by Japanese armored cars. Seeing the train derail, the bandits swarmed onto the train. Their weapons were new and effective, rarely seen among ordinary bandits. After boarding, they searched passengers for valuables, carrying them off the train. They also selected several laborers from the passengers to carry their stolen goods before leaving the railway. Upon receiving the report, the Railway Bureau quickly dispatched eighty railway police officers from Dahu Shan to pursue the bandits. Troop trains from the 19th Brigade also arrived at Dahu Shan, awaiting orders to proceed. Simultaneously, Japanese soldiers dispatched an armored train from Huanggu Tun to the scene. By the time the train arrived, the bandits had dispersed, taking only the six foreigners. They did not rescue the remaining passengers. The armored train retreated first. After the Railway Bureau's rescue train arrived, Japanese soldiers brought the foreigners they had taken to board the rescue train and return to Huanggu Tun. By the time the railway police arrived, the bandits were long gone, making pursuit impossible. It has been investigated that within the three hundred or so miles between Dahu Shan and Shenyang, there have been repeated machine-gun and bombing attacks by Japanese aircraft in recent days. Japanese troops also seized firearms from escort guards and railway police. The railway police officer Fan of Train No. 103 was bound and detained by Japanese troops for half a day, only to be released after being stabbed multiple times in the face with bayonets, destroying his eyebrows and eyes. Consequently, within three hundred miles east of Dahu Shan, the railway police dare not use armed patrols, leaving the bandits unchecked and causing this tragedy. The Railway Bureau was ordered to expedite the repair of the damaged track and resume normal operations. However, the overturned cars are difficult to recover, so a temporary road will be built as a substitute. It is expected to be passable within the next day or two. The derailment of passenger train No. 102 yesterday blocked all incoming and outgoing trains, preventing further incidents. Japanese troops arriving at Juliu River have reached two hundred men, setting up artillery on the east mountain of Juliu River. A Japanese interpreter claimed to the Juliu River stationmaster the other day that the Japanese army had buried an electric mine under the No. 59 railway bridge east of Juliu River to defend against Chinese troops. Japanese troop trains entered the Juliu River station without the permission of the Beining Railway. The Railway Bureau's Transportation Director, a British man named Mr. Stealey, lodged a serious protest with the Japanese Consul in Shenyang on the 24th, but had not yet received a response as of yesterday. Mr. Stealey also protested to the Japanese Consul regarding the shooting of trains by Japanese aircraft on the 24th and 25th. The Japanese Consul replied that the Japanese army had not engaged in shooting trains and requested Mr. Stealey to provide evidence of Japanese aircraft shooting trains. Yesterday, Mr. Stealey specially transported the bodies of passengers killed by Japanese

Page 10

aircraft to Huanggu Tun, taking photos as evidence. Mr. Stealey's first protest letter is as follows: "Sir, I am instructed by the director to lodge a serious protest with your consulate regarding the deployment of two Japanese military trains carrying troops and weapons to the Juliu River and Xinmin stations last night (i.e., the evening of the 23rd). A Japanese officer contacted me, requesting permission for two military trains to proceed to the Juliu River along our railway line. This train was already on our railway line outside Huanggu Tun station. I immediately replied that this could not be done and that I would telegraph the director to ask for instructions and reply promptly. The officer and other accompanying officers and soldiers then left without my permission, and the train proceeded to Juliu River and Xinmin, setting up artillery on the Juliu River platform, while the armored train remained at Xinmin East Station. Accordingly, I request your Consul-General to promptly forward the protest of the Beining Railway authorities to the Japanese Commander-in-Chief." (27th)

Liaoning Provincial Government to be Temporarily Established in Jinzhou 71

Beiping Communication: Following the announcement of Mi Chunlin's appointment as Acting Chairman of the Liaoning Provincial Government, preparations for organization are underway in Beiping. Simultaneously, the Deputy Commander's Headquarters has also designated specialists to investigate the Shenyang government officials who have sought refuge in Beiping. The current members of the Liaoning Provincial Government in Beiping include Xing Tulin, Huang Xiansheng, Peng Jiqun, and Zhang Zhenlu. The remaining are yet to be known. Officials from various provincial government agencies began reporting yesterday and are scheduled to depart for Jin County today or tomorrow with the former provincial committee members in Beiping to establish the provincial government's administrative office. All supplies are being procured in Beiping by Huang Jianqiu, who is rushing to complete them by last night. It is rumored that Zhu Guangmu will also travel to Jin County on the same train to discuss everything with Zhang Zuoxiang.

Yesterday morning at eleven o'clock, I visited Mi Chunlin, the Acting Chairman of the Liaoning Provincial Government. I was granted an audience. According to Mr. Mi, he received the order to act as chairman the other night and immediately began preparations. Currently, the four committee members, Xing, Zhang, Peng, and Huang, are all in Beiping and will proceed to Jin County in the next few days to establish the provincial government. Mr. Mi stated that he would postpone his departure to handle some remaining affairs at the arsenal. The number of secretaries and other staff below the department chiefs in the provincial government in Beiping is currently under investigation and not yet fully known. The areas of Liaoning Province that have been occupied need not be discussed. The security and finances of the counties that have not been occupied by the Japanese army urgently need to be managed to sustain the livelihood of the people. Therefore, after the establishment of the provincial government, the Finance Department and the Police Department will be established first. Department Chief Zhang (Zhenlu) and Director Huang (Xiansheng) are both former officials and will find it easier to handle. The organization of the Shenyang municipal government will be postponed for the time being. Chairman Zhang (Zuoxiang) is still in Jin County overseeing everything and plans to make a trip to Jilin. Yu Zhen has also been released and returned home, etc. Next, I inquired about the current state of the arsenal. He said that because the factory stores ammunition, it cannot move guns, so there was no resistance. There were many Japanese engineers in the factory, so the takeover was peaceful. If it had caused an explosion of ammunition, Shenyang would not have been safe, so neither side opened fire. Currently, the finished products stored in the factory have all been transported away by the Japanese army. (27th)

Executive Yuan

41st State Council Meeting 72

Reorganization of Shanxi Provincial Government

Xu Yongchang Appointed as Chairman

The Executive Yuan held its 41st State Council meeting on the 29th. Present were Song Ziwen, Ma Fuxiang, and Lian Shenghai. The following matters were discussed: (1) The Guizhou Provincial Government submitted a report stating that its Department of Industry was reorganized from the former Department of Agriculture and Mining and only handles agricultural and mining affairs. All industrial and commercial affairs are still temporarily handled by the Department of Construction. To facilitate overall planning and save expenses, it is proposed to abolish the Department of Industry and merge it into the Department of Construction. It is appropriate to submit this for review and forward it to the National Government for record. The decision was approved. (2) The decision was made to reorganize the Shanxi Provincial Government and to appoint Xu Yongchang, Meng Wenyuan, Qiu Zengi, Miao Peicheng, Tian Jianlong, Chang Bingyi, Hu Yiling, Li Shangren, and Ma Jun as members of the Shanxi Provincial Government, with Xu Yongchang as Chairman, Meng Wenyuan concurrently as Director of the Department of Civil Affairs, Qiu Zengi concurrently as Director of the Department of Finance, Miao Peicheng concurrently as Director of the Department of Education, Chang Bingyi concurrently as Director of the Department of Industry, and Tian Jianlong concurrently as Director of the Department of Construction.

Local Communication

Songjiang 73

Fraudulent Investigation of Enemy Goods Exposed: Ye Songzhi, a resident outside the north gate of this county, recently encountered Wang Yizhou, an Yixing native claiming to be a clerk from the Construction Bureau, who stated that Shoupin Zhi had filed a complaint alleging encroachment on the official river and that he was specially ordered to investigate and respond. After speaking, he left. The Ye family then inquired at the Construction Bureau and learned that the bureau had no clerk named Wang, nor was there any complaint filed. There was no case of the director ordering an investigation. They were instructed to pay attention. Later, someone informed Ye that the case could be resolved by giving two hundred yuan. Ye feigned acceptance and scheduled the delivery for yesterday morning. At the appointed time, Wang arrived as scheduled. Ye first handed over five ten-yuan banknotes from the Bank of China, promising to pay the balance later. Ye waited until Wang put the banknotes into his pocket before sending someone to summon the police, who arrested Wang Yizhou, who was extorting money under a false name, and brought him to the First Sub-Precinct of the Public Security Bureau. Ye stated that the banknotes were all stamped with overlapping seals, with the numbers recorded, and could be verified. After the banknotes and official documents were found on Wang's person and confirmed to be authentic, Wang Yizhou confessed that his real name was Zhou Yuqing, that he was falsely working as a secretary on the highway, and that he had been fooled for a moment. He begged for leniency. He was immediately sent to the main bureau for preliminary interrogation and a document was prepared to transfer him to the prosecutor's office for investigation and prosecution.

Inspection of Enemy Goods Measures: The Anti-Japanese National Salvation Committee of this county held its second committee meeting yesterday (28th) to discuss matters. Recently, the committee received reports that many shops in the city were secretly importing Japanese goods. The question was how to handle this matter. It was resolved to designate registration forms and send them to the Chamber of Commerce for distribution. All daily postal packages must be inspected before distribution. Personnel will be dispatched daily to inspect stations and wharves, first establishing a postal inspection team with four members each, filled by directors and members of the inspection division. The case of Zhuang Hongda secretly importing Japanese goods will be thoroughly investigated by Zhang Yiyun, a member of the Standing Committee of the committee, together with Dai Kunpei, director of the inspection division, before further action is taken.

Suzhou 74

Appealed Verdict in Guan Daming Case: Guan Daming, the owner of the Shanghai Gaotian Yanghang shoe store, was sentenced by the Shanghai District Court to three years and six months in prison for raping Zheng Xuanying. Guan refused to accept the verdict and appealed to the High Court. After repeated trials and debates, the court rendered its verdict yesterday (29th), overturning the original verdict and declaring Guan Daming innocent.

Ancient Building Discovered in Hu Guan Township: Ding Nanzhou, the district head of the first district of Hu Shu Guan, inspected Qiuzhuang Bridge Township. While passing through the eastern foothills of Yangshan, he found chalk mines and discovered an ancient brick-built long corridor, very tall and grand. It was definitely an ancient building, but it had been dug into two sections. The starting and ending points were still in the mountains and had not been excavated. Whether it was an ancient tomb or a Liao Dynasty road was impossible to determine due to the soil cover. As the matter concerns an ancient building, whether it is subject to the Ancient Artifacts Protection Law and whether it is necessary to preserve it was specially reported to the county for review yesterday (29th).

Wuxi 75

Experimental Teacher Generously Joins the Army: Cao Mengliang, a fourth-grade teacher at the Experimental Primary School of the Provincial Wuxi Middle School, actively participated in the anti-Japanese national salvation movement after the Shenyang Incident. Upon hearing that the volunteer army organized by various universities in Beijing and Shanghai, he resolutely abandoned his pen and joined the army. The other night, he wrote a letter to Zhu Nianhe, the head of the Experimental School, and his colleagues, stating that he had dedicated himself to the party and the country, vowing to wash away the national humiliation and refusing to live a life of ease. He left that evening. Afterward, Zhu and others learned of this and were unable to find him. They believed that as a primary school teacher, he had his own way to save the country and did not need to join the army. Jiang Zhida and other friends have telegraphed classmates in Beijing and Shanghai, asking them to help find him.

Jiangyin 76

Nanjing Students Organize National Salvation Student Union: The Nanjing students, outraged by the atrocities committed by the Japanese, who invaded our Eastern Provinces and killed our soldiers and civilians, convened a meeting of officers the other day to organize a volunteer corps. On the 26th, the association established a special National Salvation Committee to discuss action plans. (1) The association will establish two directors, dividing tasks into five departments: general affairs, text propaganda, oral propaganda, preparation for the National Salvation Volunteer Corps, and documentation. Each department will elect two directors. (2) At eight o'clock on the morning of the 27th, all students will depart in teams to publicize the truth about the Japanese atrocities. (3) The high school students will form a student army, the junior high school students will form a boy scout group, and the female students will form a nursing corps, all combined into the National Salvation Volunteer Corps, with training scheduled to begin next week. (4) Using the Nanjing Student Self-Government Association as the center, connect with various schools to organize a student union and convene representatives from various schools on the 28th to discuss action plans.

All Circles Brave Rain to Hold Anti-Japanese National Salvation Congress: The county party department's propaganda committee convened all circles to prepare for an anti-Japanese national salvation mass meeting, which was held at the public sports field yesterday (28th) at nine o'clock in the morning. Attendance was high. Despite the heavy rain, the meeting proceeded, with aroused public sentiment, tragic enthusiasm, unlike any previous mass meeting. After the meeting, there was a parade, and telegrams were sent to the central party department, the national government, and compatriots across the country, unanimously advocating the extermination of the Japanese devils without hesitation. They immediately organized a volunteer army, training day and night, as a support for the government. At the same time, they advocated economic sanctions against Japan, strictly enforcing the ban without any leniency.

Bengbu 80

Bengbu Holds Anti-Japanese Citizens' Congress: Since the Japanese invasion and occupation of the territory of our Eastern Provinces, the massacre of our officials, soldiers, and civilians, and the looting of our weapons and property, although the League of Nations has notified them to withdraw their troops, the Japanese government has not complied. The Japanese army continues to occupy and massacre with violence. People from all walks of life here are extremely indignant and specially held an anti-Japanese national salvation citizens' congress in Bengshan Martyrs' Park on the morning of the 27th at ten o'clock. Representatives of various agencies and groups, as well as military police, students, and citizens, attended the meeting, totaling more than ten thousand people. The atmosphere was extremely tense. After the chairman reported the opening of the meeting, Li Wenbin, the brigade commander of the 21st Brigade of the Seventh Division, and Peng Zhuoru, the representative of the Chamber of Commerce, delivered speeches in succession. The main points were nothing more than uniting together to face the national crisis, resisting Japan and saving the country, and severing economic ties. Afterward, the district party department proposed two motions: (1) The congress telegraphed to the people of the whole country to unanimously resist Japan under the leadership of the Central Committee. (2) Notify the Bengbu Anti-Japanese Aid to Overseas Chinese Committee in the name of the congress to strictly implement economic sanctions. All motions were passed on the spot and the meeting was adjourned at about twelve o'clock.

Teachers and Students of National Central University Petition the Ministry of Foreign Affairs 81

Principal Zhu Requests Dismissal

Submits Memorial Stating He Insulted Wang Zhengting

Teachers, students, and others from National Central University, upon hearing the bad news of Japan's sudden dispatch of troops and invasion of our country's Northeast territory, were extremely indignant. The entire body of teachers and all students organized the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association and actively engaged in anti-Japanese activities. At seven o'clock in the morning on the 28th, a plenary meeting was held in the auditorium of the university, deciding to petition the Central Party Department, the National Government, and the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and deciding to request the following eight points, all of which were passed unanimously. After the adjournment, Professor He Haoruo, the chairman of the meeting, led the procession. At nine o'clock, they arrived at the Central Party Department, where representatives entered to petition. The entire mass stood solemnly in good order. Subsequently, Committee Member Ding Weifen responded in the rain, and the procession continued to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs. The ranks gathered outside the door, and representatives were elected to visit Foreign Minister Wang. Because Foreign Minister Wang hid and refused to meet, the public sentiment was even more aroused. The number of people was extremely crowded, and the place was narrow, resulting in conflicts with Foreign Minister Wang. The situation at the time was quite tense. Finally, Commander-in-Chief He Haoruo led the entire group to the National Government to petition. The road was drenched with heavy rain, but the procession remained extremely orderly. After arriving at the National Government, Chairman Jiang and Dean Yu received them, resulting in a very satisfactory outcome. The entire group returned to school at twelve thirty. It is heard that the university's Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association will continue to actively pursue its activities, vowing to fight the Japanese imperialists to the end. The eight points requested are as follows: (1) Request the government to immediately facilitate peaceful unification. (2) Request the government to issue an ultimatum to Japan and actively prepare for war. (3) Request the government to dismiss Wang Zhengting. (4) Request the government to clearly order the restoration of the popular movement. (5) Request the government to earnestly implement national military training. (6) Request the government to quickly appoint competent diplomats to fill the vacant ambassadorial positions in various countries to facilitate diplomacy. (7) Request the government to hold the frontier commanders accountable for their responsibilities to defend the territory. (8) Request the government to vigorously implement national diplomacy.

Zhu Jiahua Submits Memorial Requesting Punishment

Yesterday (28th), teachers and students of National Central University paraded and petitioned at the Ministry of Foreign Affairs regarding the Japanese troop deployment, which resulted in a slight dispute. Principal Zhu admitted that his handling was inadequate and specially submitted a resignation to the Ministry of Education. The resignation is recorded below:

Submits this memorial to request dismissal and punishment. This morning, all teachers and students of the school jointly petitioned the Central Party Department, the National Government, and the Ministry of Foreign Affairs. Suddenly, other elements joined along the way, resulting in a noisy crowd. When arriving at the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, the order suddenly broke down, resulting in insults to Minister Wang and damage to public property of the ministry. Upon hearing the news, Jiahua was extremely terrified. As the principal, Jiahua's handling was inadequate, resulting in this unfortunate incident, and he should bear all responsibility. Accordingly, I respectfully request your department to approve my dismissal and impose a severe punishment. I am waiting urgently for your order. Respectfully submitted to the Ministry of Education, Zhu Jiahua, Principal of National Central University.

Extension of Approval for Private Middle School Registration in Beiping Approved 82

Until the Day Before the Start of the Second Semester of the 20th Year

The Beiping Municipal Education Bureau previously submitted to the Ministry of Education, stating that the Ministry of Education's order regarding the deadline for the registration of six private schools, schools above the college level, was extended to the end of January of the 20th year, and schools below the middle school level, except for provinces and cities where the registration procedures were nearing completion, should follow the previous order and be handled by the competent departments to determine the extension period and submit it for approval, but it could not be delayed beyond the end of June of the 21st year. Furthermore, private schools that have been registered should be managed conscientiously, and newly established schools should not recruit students without authorization before being approved for establishment, and violators should be dealt with according to regulations, etc. However, it has been found that this city is a cultural center, and there are many private schools below the middle school level. Some have already followed the regulations and applied for registration, but there are still many that have not registered. Moreover, due to military transportation interruptions last year, the Ministry of Education's instructions were not known until March of this year. Although urged, review and correction would take time, and it may be difficult to complete the procedures on schedule. If they are terminated upon expiration, there will inevitably be regrets. It is proposed to request approval for an extension until the day before the start of the second semester of the 20th year to facilitate supervision and management. The Ministry of Education instructed that the submission be noted and handled as proposed.

County Education Bureau Meeting 85

The Shanghai County Education Bureau held its 128th bureau affairs meeting yesterday. Those in attendance were Bureau Chief Shi, Supervisor Zhu, Zheng Zhai, Yang Huiming, Lin Wenwen, Niu Zhiyi, Ling Sansheng, Qian Zhonghou, and Yan Chongguang. The meeting was chaired by Bureau Chief Shi and recorded by Ling Sansheng. It was resolved that the budget for the 20th year had already been established, and the county's total tuition income was over seven thousand yuan. Waiving the fees would make it impossible for the bureau to raise funds to compensate, making it difficult to comply. (2) The tenant of the two-story building in Qiuwei, Zhang Ming, has been in arrears of rent for eleven months and has repeatedly failed to pay despite reminders. What should be done? It was resolved that he should pay the arrears by the end of the month; otherwise, the building will be taken back and rented to someone else. (3) The County Education Association requested the establishment of an Education Achievement Exhibition Room. It was resolved that preparations would be made after the relocation of the government. (4) In the past, parental education funds in each district were received and distributed by the Education Committee together with the district chiefs. However, at the end of the year, incomplete receipts caused difficulties in preparing the final accounts. How should this be handled? It was resolved that, in addition to informing the Education Committees, the county government should instruct the district chiefs to submit the receipts from each school for the previous month when coming to the bureau to receive their funds in the future, before they can receive the funds for the current month. The meeting was adjourned.

Shanghai Student Representatives Talk

Details of the Petition to Chiang in Beijing 87

Chiang Expresses that the Central Government Will Absolutely Not Let Down the Nation

Dai Jitao Says the Government Bears Full Responsibility

Riri News Agency reports: The Shanghai University Students Anti-Japanese National Salvation Federation's petition delegation, totaling representatives from various universities in Shanghai, boarded a train on the evening of the 25th of this month to go to Beijing to petition for five demands, including punishing diplomatic officials and Northeast military personnel, issuing firearms to students, and declaring war on Japan. They received satisfactory replies from Chairman Chiang of the National Government and President Dai Jitao. They have now returned to Shanghai and yesterday reported in detail to Riri News Agency reporters about their petition. The details are as follows:

This trip involved a delegation of 56 people from 26 schools. They departed from Shanghai at 11:30 PM on the 25th, arrived in Beijing at 8:00 AM on the 26th, and stayed at National Central University. At 10:30 AM that morning, they went to the National Government to petition. They met Chairman Chiang in the auditorium, who gave them satisfactory answers to the five demands. The discussion lasted for two hours before they left. On the morning of the 27th, they went to the Central Party Headquarters, where they were received by Minister Chen Lifu. In the afternoon, they visited the mausoleum and hosted reporters. In the evening, they visited Hu Hanmin. On the morning of the 28th at 7:00 AM, they decided to return to Shanghai. At 9:00 AM that morning, they attended the Central Party Headquarters' memorial week. They met Dai Jitao in the first conference room of the Central Party Headquarters, who, on behalf of the Central Government, responded to the students' demands. In the afternoon, they boarded a train and arrived in Shanghai at midnight yesterday.

Chiang's Expression: Chairman Chiang's address to the Shanghai university students stated briefly that the students did not seem to fully understand the government, but it was necessary to know that the government was actively working to deal with the Japanese. When the students asked Chiang to respond to the five demands, Chiang addressed the first demand, to declare war on Japan, by saying that when there was absolutely no possibility of peace, troops would ultimately have to be sent to fight to the death. Regarding the second demand, to punish Wang Zhengting, he replied that diplomatic failures should be the full responsibility of the government and not the responsibility of one person. Regarding the third demand, to order Zhang Xueliang to quickly reclaim the lost territory and atone for his crimes, he replied that the student representatives did not need to worry about this point and that the Central Government would certainly have to take back the territory, while atonement for his crimes was a matter for the future. Regarding the fourth demand, to issue firearms to students, he replied that there was a shortage of firearms in the country and that for every firearm a student had, a soldier would have one less. Therefore, it was difficult to do so for the time being. In the future, at the appropriate time, students would certainly be able to obtain firearms. Now, they could concentrate on receiving military training. The Central Government did not want students to go to war because students were the knowledgeable youth of the country and would be the pillars of the country in the future. If all the students sacrificed themselves for the country, this kind of loss would be extremely significant. The government would not send students out to defend the country unless it was absolutely necessary. Regarding the fifth demand, not to sign treaties that forfeit rights and humiliate the country and to make diplomacy public, Chiang replied that this was even more the Central Government's responsibility. The Central Government must take the will of the people as its will, and diplomacy should also be absolutely public.

Dai's Expression: When the student delegation went to petition, Dai Jitao also responded to the five demands one by one, stating briefly that diplomatic failures were the responsibility of the government and that the government would not fail the expectations of the people. The government would never use diplomacy to seek personal gain. Chen Lifu also gave earnest advice to the students, which the student representatives considered satisfactory, and they then returned to Shanghai.

Hu Hanmin's Remarks: Hu Hanmin was ill at home. The representatives went to his home to present their cards and request an audience. Hu was upstairs due to his illness, fearing exposure to the cold. He could not come out to see them, so he asked the representatives to enter his bedroom. Hu said that the occurrence of this incident was planned by the Japanese beforehand and was not accidental. He was still seriously ill and had not yet recovered, so it was difficult for him to come out of retirement for the time being. However, he would still devote himself to national affairs and would immediately report any methods to the Central Government for adoption. Hu also encouraged the students to implement economic severance with Japan in the future. The youth themselves should also pay attention to organization and propaganda.

The Sixth District Education Association Holds Anti-Japanese Rally 88

Many Measures to Deal with the Brutal Japanese Decided

Representatives to Attend the City Education Association Meeting Also Elected

The Sixth District Education Association of this city held a membership meeting yesterday at the Sanmin School on Baoxing Road, Zhabei, to discuss anti-Japanese work and elect representatives to attend the City Education Association meeting. Despite the heavy rain, members paid their fees to attend enthusiastically. (C) Each school should designate and make armbands with maps of national humiliation and distribute them to students to wear, so that they will never forget. Declaration of the Vocational Guidance Federation 95

The Chinese Vocational Guidance Organization Federation recently made the following declaration: Against reason and abandoning justice, violating the Kellogg-Briand Pact, advancing troops into the eastern provinces, and brutally killing our national compatriots. The whole country is filled with sorrow and anger, and the world is holding grievances. Our colleagues in the education sector are deeply saddened by this national crisis. In the aftermath of pain, they should plan self-rescue and save the country. It is generally believed that this association is a vocational guidance group. The establishment of round arguments emphasizes the promotion of spiritual education, the cultivation of strength, attention to production education, and the enrichment of people's livelihoods as two major guidelines. Regarding the main surface of production education, the complete implementation of economic severance, the increase of national production, and the perpetual non-use of Japanese goods are the main purposes, in order to resist brutal Japan and develop the people's livelihood as the fundamental plan. Current work (1) Investigate the types, quantities, and values ​​of imported Japanese goods. (2) Investigate whether there are domestic goods that can replace the above-mentioned Japanese goods, what factory produces the domestic goods, and what is the value. (3) Establish domestic goods exhibition halls or domestic goods markets in various places, and display Japanese goods next to each domestic goods for comparison. (4) Based on the investigation results, engage in the creation and improvement of domestic goods factories. (9) Based on the results of the investigation, extensively publicize and advise on the use of domestic goods, so that all compatriots in the country will know the danger of using Japanese goods. Regarding spiritual education, 1. Young men and women should actively pay attention to physical exercise and implement military training. 2. Reject bad habits and cultivate a sound and good personality. 3. Pay attention to self-cultivation and strive for the improvement of one's own business. 4. Devote oneself to academics, research the improvement and invention of items, in order to achieve the purpose of saving the country through science. The people of the country must know that in this world where justice is not judged, it is better to seek oneself than to seek others. Relying on others is not worthwhile. At this time of national crisis, in addition to the concerted efforts of the whole country to actively prepare for war, the compatriots of all industries can only bury their heads in business, intensify their work, in order to seek the development of affairs and the increase of industry. With one point of spirit, do one point of career, more one point of work, increase one point of strength, and look forward to the compatriots of the whole country, who are usually long in serving all walks of life, and once there is a disaster, everyone will hold Ge to defend the country. If things come to this point, destruction is not far away. Today, there is absolutely no reason for our people to live in peace, compromise, or fluke. I respectfully offer it and hope you will take it into consideration.

Postponement of Next Year's World Games

Most European Countries Agree... Affected by the Global Economic Recession 100

Los Angeles News: Currently, all countries in the world are affected by the economic recession, resulting in economic panic in various countries. It was recently rumored that the 10th World Games, which will be held in the United States next year, may be suspended. The truth has now been clarified. This matter was proposed by Sweden because, in view of the world's situation, all countries do not have sufficient capacity to send athletes. For example, French athletes have to raise their own travel expenses. Britain and Germany are also struggling with finances and tend not to participate. Therefore, it is proposed to postpone the conference, otherwise the conference will be reduced. Sweden's proposal was subsequently supported by most European countries. However, the president of the World Sports Association, the American Foer Lanzhi, stated that Sweden's proposal will now be sent to the countries by the conference to solicit their consent. If more than half of the countries agree to the postponement, the conference must be postponed and held in the next session. However, the Los Angeles venue has been properly arranged. If the conference is postponed, the losses suffered by the United States will be indescribable.

Free Talk

Heartbreaking Words 101

— Du Juan

Dear compatriots, is our Republic of China dead? Is it already the second India? India has already perished, and under heavy oppression every day, it has lost all freedom and has no way to resist. Therefore, it adopted the method of non-violent resistance. Now our non-resistance to Japan is so similar. However, where is Gandhi? Where is Gandhi? Heaven, please give us a Gandhi.

Unremoving Garden Grass Studio Husband's Conversational Collection

Defeated But Still Fighting 102

When Zeng Guofan suffered several defeats, his staff drafted a memorial for him with the words "repeatedly defeated in battle." He picked up his pen and crossed it out, turning it into "defeated but still fighting," and his spirits were lifted. A coward who could not even catch a chicken could immediately be transformed into a hero who could resist a hundred enemies after seeing this stroke.

Whenever I encounter an incident, I always treat it with the attitude of solving a mathematical problem, using a calm mind to guide the path of my boiling blood, so I rarely feel indignation and rarely feel pessimistic. However, since the fall of Shenyang, every time I see Zhang Xueliang's telegrams, I cannot help but feel angry. In these telegrams, all I see is the fall, withdrawal, death and injury, and disarmament, and I do not see any expression of great fearless spirit. This is cold water poured on the flames of national spirit. If you fight and are defeated, the people will forgive you. If you are defeated and fight again, the people will respect you. If you fight and are defeated, and you are defeated and do not fight, the people will one day settle accounts with you. Because what you have lost is not just land, but the spirit of establishing a country. You still have a chance to atone for your crimes. If you miss it, it is such a pity!

Poem on National Humiliation 103

— Chen Zhuzun

In the ninth month of the twentieth year, on the nineteenth day at dawn, Japanese soldiers recklessly committed violence, seizing my Fengtian City. Jilin was subsequently captured, and disaster will come to Beiping. They replaced my officials and killed my people. Bad news came from the Northeast, and the people lamented in shock. They began to wake up from their dreams, and compatriots called out to each other as brothers. Why do bean stalks hate each other? Why are they so eager to cook each other? National hatred is abandoned, and party resentment is unclear. The caller's voice is already hoarse, but who can hear? Only allowing unarmed scholars to talk about weapons on paper. Slogans are written in red and green but cannot be fought. How can cunning enemies know that troops will come to the city without declaring war? Annexing my three provinces is still called a local act. I heard that the officials of the three provinces raised many elite troops. They were said to number hundreds of thousands, allowing them to act recklessly in the Northeast. They won against Cao Wu in one fell swoop, and defeated You and Bing in the second. They annihilated the rebellious Shi in the third and played the triumph with joyful voices. The pride of China, the Great Wall of North China. How can they be plowed by enemies in a moment? Like destroying dead wood and rotten grass, like cutting fresh flesh and cooking sacrifices. Beating dogs into poor alleys, struggling to resist each other desperately. How can they be worse than dogs, retreating regardless of the distance. The central army is mighty and glorious, and the conquests are like gods. They wiped out Li Bai in one fell swoop and overthrew Feng Tang in the second. They suppressed the Red bandits in the third and then marched south. How can the central government enjoy fighting? It is necessary to protect its prestige. The general's spirit is overwhelming, how can the hundred Yue be leveled? Focusing on punishing rebels, vowing not to live under the same sky. The prestige is spread, flashing like thunder. Why do enemies come without even welcoming a soldier? The city fell for three or four days, and no angry voice was heard. Where is the credibility now? The promises are just filling the court. Recalling the things of the past, only wanting to decorate peace. Concealing the illness and avoiding medical treatment, disaster even reached this point. The country has been in decline for a long time, why wait until now to understand? The greatest thing is the death of the heart, and tears flow as I speak. The country has raised warriors for twenty years. The annual consumption is tens of millions, and there are flags everywhere. Why be afraid of public war but brave in private disputes? Years of civil strife, killings are incessant. Borrowing money to buy foreign weapons, the ambitions are all proud and arrogant. The military is divided into the sea, land, and air, and the three parties fight each other. Rivers and valleys flow with human blood, and cities and suburbs become hills. Now the war has not yet ended, what else is there to do? I fear that in a few days, it will end in a city alliance. Otherwise, the Russo-Japanese War will involve world soldiers. Death will have no burial place, how dare I hope to steal life? I wish all the people of the country would wake up from their dreams at the same time. I also wish the loyal warriors to carefully weigh the pros and cons of fortune. The country will be slaves together, and wealth is not your glory. Abandon resentment early and plan for the country's rejuvenation. I also wish the young warriors to not be frivolous in their intentions. Focus on studying knowledge and stop the sacrifice of skipping classes. Reading breaks ten thousand volumes and brings peace to the country. The past is dead yesterday, and the future is born today. Ten years of livelihood and accumulation, ten years of education and training. All studies are advanced, scholars, farmers, workers, and soldiers. Each fulfills their duties, as brothers to each other. Maybe we can wash away the national humiliation, and the bamboo slips will record our achievements. I bow my head nine times after writing the poem, please appreciate my sincerity.

The Wonderful Child on the Zhangpu Gate 104

— Qingqu

The Ming Dynasty pirates harassed our coastal borders, and my county of Xiding was often in danger. The city was captured several times. On April 16 of the 33rd year of Jiajing, the bandits arrived in force and surrounded the county seat again. At that time, the neighboring states and counties were all invaded and had no time to save themselves. Yin Fenglin, the county magistrate, was a professor in the prefecture and served as the county magistrate. He was also panicked and did not know what to do. The scholars and people discussed and decided to divide the city walls and take self-defense measures. On the morning of that day, the bandits approached the city and plundered the countryside during the day and set fires at night. Cries of lamentation were everywhere, and corpses were piled up into burial mounds. One evening, the bandits approached the West Gate and had already climbed the city wall. The guards were sleeping soundly, so they climbed up the ladder and reached the parapet. A child saw it by chance with a lamp under the city and then shouted loudly. The crowd was startled and woke up, and they hurriedly threw stones and broke the ladder, causing the bandits to retreat. However, looking down at the child, his head had fallen to the ground, and the smell of blood touched the nose. Later, Yang Song, a Henan native, was in the county and killed hundreds of bandits successively. They held out for a month before the bandits fled. The authorities were grateful for the child's courage and bravery and the bandits' schemes and unanimously decided to carve a stone statue. When the statue was completed, it faced east and sat on the city gate. It still exists today. The West Gate is located in Zhangpu, so it is named He Pu Gate. It is a pity that the county chronicles did not record the child's surname and he became an anonymous hero. However, compared to the current invasion by the violent Japanese and the axes of the north and south, which have been sitting idly by, it is said that they own four hundred million people, advocating the overthrow of imperialism, and everyone is in the position of master, but they also allow thieves to enter the room and ransack my treasures. Then they were shocked and stunned and blamed the guards for their carelessness. Why are they not as good as the child? Alas, I can't bear to say it anymore.

Record of a Deaf Man's Lecture and Hearing 105

— Ren Peichu

The Chinese Christian Youth Association invited Dr. Schukat to give a lecture on the evening of September 25th, titled "How to Reduce the Suffering of the Deaf." That evening, I happened to visit a friend at the Youth Association and took the opportunity to attend the lecture. I have recorded it below.

The Suffering of the Deaf: Schukat said, "I (Schukat referring to himself) am a researcher of philosophy, not a medical researcher. I have absolutely no understanding of the treatment of deafness. However, because I have been an elderly deaf person with decades of hearing loss, I deeply understand the suffering of the deaf, which is greater than that of the blind and mute. Although blindness is painful, everyone can tell at a glance that the person is disabled, and they cannot help but feel pity. Mutes have mouths but cannot speak, so disaster does not befall them. Deaf people, on the other hand, show no signs of disability in their appearance, and when talking to others, they often become entangled and clash in their speech, leading to insults from the other party. Sometimes, it can even stir up a major storm. Furthermore, if a deaf person is walking on the road and is unfortunately hit by a car, the driver will inevitably use excuses such as having repeatedly honked the horn and the vehicle being unable to stop in time. If it were not a deaf person, they could point out the driver's lies. At this time, the deaf person has no words to defend themselves. Is this not suffering?"

Organizing a Federation: The benefits that deaf people enjoy in society only account for 40% of those of ordinary people. Anything that requires hearing is not their share. Life is really very boring. The best way to remedy this is to organize a deaf federation. The federation should include a club and a job placement office. The former is for the entertainment of the deaf, and the latter is to help the deaf find a livelihood. This way, the loneliness of the deaf can be reduced.

Special Listening Style: Eight out of ten of the listeners that day were fellow deaf people. At first, they only cupped their hands behind their ears to aid hearing. Later, because the sound waves still could not reach their ears, they gradually left their seats and went towards the podium. Finally, all the deaf people gathered around the podium, surrounding the elderly deaf Dr. Schukat in the center. However, the deaf people still felt it was not enough and continued to cup their hands behind their ears.

Mr. Chen Gan-yi, the Master of the Dhi Xiang Studio, turned forty on the seventeenth day of the eighth lunar month. He has linked together the five-character couplet by Mr. Yu Youren, "His literary talent startles all who sit with him," and "By not serving, he strengthens his body." And Mr. Luo Fukan's collected verse, "True strength

The Sound of Patriotic Songs in a Time of National Crisis: A Public Awareness Campaign Through Music 107

— Xu Wancheng

"Sonification" refers to using music to inspire the people. Music can best harmonize and beautify everything in the universe. Confucius said, "Music is the harmony of the world... Harmony is why the world is transformed." Sima Qian said, "Music is that by which the pulse is moved, the spirit is circulated, and the heart is harmonized." Wilhelm II said, "Music is enough to transform the evil and decadent souls of mankind, making them pure, passionate, and increasingly upward." Beethoven said, "Sublime and great personalities, the thoughts of sages, and the achievements that cover the world can only be formed and cultivated through the refinement of music."

In short, "Music is the art of expressing emotion." As the saying goes, "One tragic song can move thousands to tears." In the past, when Guan Zhong assisted Duke Huan of Qi and led his troops on a distant expedition, the soldiers found it difficult to climb the steep mountain ridges. Guan Zhong composed the song "It is difficult to climb the mountain, but easy to descend." They sang it back and forth, and the sound of the song echoed through the clouds. The soldiers' extreme fatigue was relieved by the song. Also, during the Chu-Han contention, Xiang Yu was trapped at Gaixia (now southeast of Lingbi County, Anhui). Zhang Zifang's song with the flute caused the Chu army's morale to collapse. From this, it is known that music deeply inspires the masses and has the power to change personal emotions.

All countries in the world attach importance to "music." The United States will hold a joint conference of national musicians, poets, and writers in Chicago in 1933. The largest church in London, Truro Cathedral, recently organized a choir with over a thousand members. Also, the city of Messiah in Germany awards 300,000 marks annually to the city's top musician.

At this time, with the autumn air crisp and the national crisis looming, the Chinese Municipal Progressive Association held a "Public Awareness Campaign Through Music for National Salvation" on the evening of September 27th. Mr. Huang Jingwan was responsible for the preparations and invited Messrs. Miao Zhijie, Chen Gexin, and Lu Danlin to assist. There were many programs that evening.

The Female Doctor's Opening Speech: Dr. Qian Jianqiu, a Doctor of Law, gave the opening speech. The main idea was "The purpose of the 'Public Awareness Campaign Through Music for National Salvation' and the understanding we should have about resisting Japan and saving the nation." Her words were very alarming. Dr. Qian also attended with her mother and Dr. Huang Biying that evening.

Wang Qingxun Put on a Great Show: That evening, Mr. Huang Qingxun, the president of the Chinese Harmonica Association, led the Chinese Harmonica Team in singing the Party Song and led the Shanghai Provincial Middle School Harmonica Team in playing "Forward Courageously." Mr. Wang also played a harmonica solo of "Heaven and Hell" and took the opportunity to give a speech. His tone was passionate, and the listeners were moved. Mr. Wang is from Taiwan and has experienced the brutality of Japanese imperialism firsthand, and his resentment filled his chest, so he had to vent it. Then he sang generously, and the audience's spirits were boosted even more.

Chen Gexin Sang with Sadness: Mr. Chen Gexin, a music professor at Shanghai Girls' High School, has an excellent voice. That evening, he sang "I Hear You Calling Me" and "My Mother" solo. They were moving and sad, and his voice lingered for three days.

Two Girls Sang Folk Songs Together: Misses Zhang Wencan and Lin Muhao, both fourteen or fifteen years old, were of equal height. Their harmonica duet of "Siamese Folk Song" was melodious and well-paced, with a lot of expressive art.

There were other programs that evening. Patriotic songs were performed, and it was a grand occasion for a while. The meeting adjourned at nine o'clock.

The Rotary Club for Storytelling

A Husband's Wife (28) 108

— Jiang Hongjiao

"No, now I have found out that the woman in the car that night was just a prostitute, and this prostitute has married someone else. This person happens to be a friend of my friend, so I know everything."

"Then what is the use of the woodenware he bought?"

"Don't be discouraged. He will definitely change his mind in the future. Not to mention anything else, like my wife, I was so discouraged before, but now..."

"Indeed, your wife is truly a husband's wife."

"So you're definitely leaving tomorrow?"

"Definitely leaving. Maybe I'll stay for three to five days to relax and then go back to Shanghai."

As Mrs. Li said this, her heart felt as if it were being cut by a knife. She reached out and shook hands with Mr. Chen, held back her tears, forced a smile, and walked back to her room.

Mrs. Chen did not return home all night, and Mr. Chen was very uneasy. He suspected that she might have been hit by a car on the road or that she might have relapsed into her old ways. However, he never suspected that her meekness for the past two months was a special act.

He pitied Mrs. Li because he dared not do anything shocking to save her, just for his own reputation and status. He also knew that Mrs. Li loved him, but she also did not have the courage to do anything shocking to remarry him. Everyone was helpless.

He did not close his eyes all night, lost in anxious thought. Mrs. Li also cried all night. But Mr. Li came home at two o'clock in the middle of the night, went to bed, and slept soundly, ignoring her.

She got up early in the morning, left a note for her husband, hurried out, and took a car to Hangzhou.

Not long after Mr. Chen got up, he suddenly received a letter from a lawyer. After he opened it, he was so angry that his hands trembled. It was a letter from a lawyer representing his wife, requesting a divorce from him.

Because the first reason stated in the letter pointed to his ambiguous relationship with Mrs. Li, he took the letter to find Mr. Li, hoping that Mr. Li could help him prove that Mrs. Li had absolutely no relationship with him.

But Mr. Li said lightly, "If a woman's heart changes, there is no turning back. A real man should not worry about having no wife. If she wants a divorce, then allow it. Now my wife has also left without saying goodbye, and maybe she will imitate your wife and send me a lawyer's letter. But I trust you very much and will never believe that you have anything to do with my wife." (The End)
