Commercial News

Financial Gold Bar Price Surge Resumes 109

Settlement Price to Adopt US Dollar Standard

Termination of Trading for Japanese Merchants

Price Increases by More Than Twenty-Eight Taels: Yesterday, the 29th, the price of gold bars showed a renewed upward trend. However, there were still twists and turns, with alternating winds and rains, making it difficult to control. People were confused and restless. In the morning session, the price fluctuated around 690 taels. In the afternoon session, it once exceeded the 700 tael mark, with a review of more than 21 taels. In the end, it surged by more than 28 taels, with buyers appearing to be in the majority. This was likely due to the fall in silver prices and, even more so, due to the intense fury of the Japanese bandits in the Northeast, causing people to feel exceptionally indignant and implement an economic boycott to resist them. Therefore, the gold industry will hold a meeting to discuss the adoption of the US dollar as the standard for settling the price of Japanese gold. The estimated price is around 827 taels and some change. After the method is discussed and decided, it can be implemented. This has already caused the market price to rise. The market opened high from the early morning, but although foreign exchange showed an increase, the difference was inconsistent, and the fluctuations were unpredictable. However, the price of gold had slight twists and turns, but the turbulence was not as great as the day before. The buying interest was even stronger in the afternoon session, causing the price to rise by more than ten taels, before briefly falling sharply.

Regulations for Securities Exchange Bond Collateral 115

Register with the Exchange First, Then Seek Collateral from Banks

Previously, bond prices plummeted, causing market turmoil. The exchange consulted with the Bank of China, the Bank of Communications, and major central banks to maintain stability. As a result, bond collateral was accepted, and under the instruction of the Ministry of Finance, the securities exchange came forward to provide collateral. The collateral methods are as follows: (1) Each broker, up to the 22nd of this month, for this month (September)'s buy transactions made on behalf of clients, if there are difficulties in delivery and receipt, the entrusted broker may be responsible for requesting registration with the exchange to pledge the purchased bonds for loans. (2) The registration procedure must be completed before 5 pm on the 26th of this month. The names and addresses of the clients, types, and quantities should be listed (excluding arbitrage) and reported to the General Affairs Section for registration and verification. (3) The aforementioned pledged bonds are of nine types (treasury bonds must be accompanied by interest coupons for the current month), and the collateral discount is calculated based on the book price recorded on the 24th of this month. (4) The aforementioned bond collateral is provided at 70% of the market value, with a monthly interest rate of 1.2%, and a term of three months. It is reported that the registered face value of each broker is approximately 8 million yuan. The specified collateral discounts for bonds are listed below (per 100 yuan):

Disbandment Bonds 43.00, 1921 Customs Bonds 41.00, Consolidated Tax Bonds 40.00

Customs Bonds 30.00, 1921 Relief Bonds 40.00, 1931 Customs Bonds 41.00

Reorganization Bonds 32.00, 1931 Short-Term Bonds 37.00, Salt Tax Bonds 39.00

Spot Yarn and Cotton on Delivery Day 116

650 Bales of Spot Yarn Traded

The spot yarn business is still considered good. Three parts of the spot market are experiencing shortages, and with Japan's forceful occupation of the Northeast and the escalating anti-Japanese military actions, Japanese yarn cannot be sold, making domestic yarn particularly tight. However, with a major disaster looming and the country in turmoil, credit is tightening. Severe floods are occurring in all parts of the country. If the price increases too sharply, the high prices will significantly impact actual sales. Futures yarn trading is suspended due to end-of-month delivery processing. Spot yarn purchases by various groups totaled 650 bales. Prices increased by 5 qian to 5 liang. 100 bales were imported from inland, 450 bales from Guangdong, 25 bales from Wuhu, 50 bales from Jiangxi, 225 bales from Hankou, and 50 bales from miscellaneous sources.

Slight Increase in Foreign Cotton

Spot cotton trading remains sparse, but there is still foreign cotton business. 2,600 bales of Yao cotton have been ordered. 50 pieces of Xingheng cotton at 32.00 yuan were imported from Guangdong and immediately shipped to Wuxi.

Extremely Low Yarn Delivery Volume This Month 117

In July, September standard yarn trading saw its peak with strong sales in Tianjin, reaching a high of 167.3 taels. Later, due to the poor condition of American cotton, it weakened again. A major merchant reversed from a long to a short position, and the market price broke through the 60-tael mark. Furthermore, due to the Wanbaoshan Incident, there was a boycott of inferior goods, and the market conditions increased again to over 164 taels. However, major players continued to sell, suppressing the price increase. Shortly thereafter, on August 8, the US government released its cotton production estimate, resulting in a sharp drop of over 110 points, severely impacting the yarn market and causing a drop of 6 taels in one day. The lowest price seen was 148.9 taels. Subsequently, a manufacturer took a long position and held it tightly. However, the global situation was exceptionally weak. Later in the middle of this month, Japan forcibly occupied the Northeast, and the anti-Japanese movement intensified, causing market conditions to suddenly rise, reaching a high of 161.1 taels. The last trade fell by 2 taels to 158.1 taels. The final delivery price was 160 taels, and the total delivery volume was 8,400 bales. However, only 150 bales were actually delivered by ten yarn merchants; the rest were self-delivered. The shortfall in this month's delivery volume is rarely seen.

Anti-Japanese National Salvation Movement Heard Yesterday 126

All Sectors Intensify Anti-Japanese Efforts

Municipal Chamber of Commerce Implements Economic Severance

Implementing Resolutions of Member Representative Conference

Severe Punishment by the People for Private Purchases

Since the Municipal Chamber of Commerce resolved various anti-Japanese national salvation measures at the Member Representative Conference the day before yesterday and swore to never again buy or sell Japanese goods, it has actively implemented the resolutions yesterday. The following are the important letters issued by the Chamber:

Notice of Complete Economic Severance with Japan The Chamber hereby notifies that for the sake of anti-Japanese national salvation, it convened a temporary Member Representative Conference on the 28th of this month and resolved that, as the Japanese are poisoning Chinese soil, occupying territory with military force, and their vicious flames are intensifying, it is urgently necessary to completely and permanently sever economic ties with Japan. Anyone who privately engages in buying or selling with Japan will be severely punished by the people upon discovery. This notice is hereby issued and recorded, and it is hoped that everyone will comply with public opinion and strictly abide by it. Anyone who outwardly complies but inwardly disobeys will be no different from inviting their own destruction and being an enemy of the country, and will inevitably become the public enemy of the entire nation. Please take note.

All Industries Should Expedite the Formation of Japanese Goods Inspection Teams The Chamber hereby notifies that for the sake of anti-Japanese national salvation, it convened a temporary Member Representative Conference on the 28th of this month and resolved that, in order to implement merchants' voluntary economic severance with Japan, all industry associations should be notified to immediately establish Japanese goods inspection teams to conduct self-inspections. If any industry association fails to establish an inspection team within one week, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce may dispatch an inspection team from another industry to conduct the inspection on its behalf. This notice is hereby issued and recorded. Please investigate and comply, and establish an inspection team within one week of receiving this letter, and report the organizational details to the Chamber for review. If the deadline is exceeded and no organization has been established or reported, the Chamber will dispatch an inspection team from another industry to conduct the inspection on its behalf. Please do not delay.

Separate Letters Sent to Various Industries Investigating the Status of Japanese Goods Yesterday, the Chamber sent letters to over thirty industry associations, including timber, western pigments, department stores, seafood groceries, seafood shops, longan materials, glass yarn industry, paper industry, cotton cloth, coal industry, and general merchandise. The Chamber hereby notifies that according to the resolution of the second plenary meeting of the Chamber's Research Committee on Resisting Japanese Goods, a Japanese goods investigation form should be prepared and distributed to various industry associations for completion and submission within ten days of receiving this letter for reference. A Japanese goods investigation form is enclosed. Please distribute it to the various merchants and instruct them to read the explanation on the form and fill in the items in detail, and submit them to the Chamber for review within one week of receiving this letter. The format of the attached investigation form is as follows: (1) Product name; (2) Type; (3) Price; (4) Source: Where is this item produced? Approximately how much is imported into our country each year? (5) Destination: What is it used for? Approximately how much is needed each year? Where is it sold? (6) Are there any substitutes? Are there any substitutes for this item? Does our country produce the same item? Does any other country produce the same item? (7) If there are other substitutes, why is this item still used? Please specify the reason.

All Associations Expedite the Formation of National Salvation Volunteer Armies The Chamber hereby notifies that for the sake of anti-Japanese national salvation, it convened a temporary Member Representative Conference on August 28 and resolved that, as the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association currently has a volunteer army organization and all schools are intensifying military training, all of our merchants should devote themselves to the battlefield and jointly face the national crisis. All industry associations should be notified to form their own national salvation volunteer armies within a limited time. This notice is hereby issued and recorded. It is hoped that your association will promptly convene fellow traders to jointly plan the organization. The methods can be handled with reference to those set by the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association. The matter concerns the national crisis and cannot be delayed or considered. The organization must be established within ten days of receiving this letter and the organizational details must be reported for review.

Letter to Banking Industry Halting Loans for Japanese Goods The Chamber hereby notifies that for the sake of anti-Japanese national salvation, it convened a temporary Member Representative Conference on the 28th of this month and resolved that, in order to implement economic severance with Japan, the banking associations should be notified to send letters to their affiliated colleagues, ordering them to immediately stop lending to merchants engaged in Japanese goods. Anyone who violates this will be deemed to be undermining the anti-Japanese movement. This letter is hereby issued and recorded. It is hoped that your association will immediately notify your colleagues to implement the meeting and implement it immediately, and please reply to the association on the handling situation for review. This is of utmost importance. To the Shanghai Banking Industry Association.

Curbing National Goods Manufacturers from Taking Advantage of the Opportunity to Raise Prices The Chamber issued a notice yesterday stating that, regarding the current Japanese atrocities, the Executive Committee resolved to convene a temporary Member Representative Conference on the 28th of this month, proposing over ten items, including "Curbing National Goods Manufacturers from Taking Advantage of the Opportunity to Raise Prices." It was unanimously resolved that, now that a permanent economic severance with Japan is being rigorously implemented, the people's daily necessities should be supplied as much as possible by national goods manufacturers, and any opportunistic price increases should be absolutely curbed to avoid losses to consumers and to create intangible resistance to Japanese goods. All national goods manufacturers are hereby notified to comply and implement this matter conscientiously to promote national goods and relieve the national crisis. This notice is hereby issued.

Looking around our country, there has been no peace since the founding of the Republic of China. Disputes have been heard daily. We hereby telegraph this message, humbly requesting your consideration and implementation. We await your orders with urgency and anticipation. The Shanghai Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association's Citizens' Assembly.

Sever Diplomatic Relations and Declare War on Japan To the Central Executive Committee of Nanjing: In order to realize its dream of a Manchurian-Mongolian policy, Japan, taking advantage of our disaster-stricken situation, suddenly sent troops to the three northeastern provinces, unreasonably occupying our important territories, burning, looting, killing, and bombing, using every means. All compatriots with blood and energy are filled with anger and hatred. Considering the urgency of foreign aggression and the precarious state of the country, the citizens of this city convened a citizens' assembly on the day before yesterday and resolved to telegraph the Central Government, demanding that the Japanese troops withdraw from the occupied territories within a limited time, otherwise, diplomatic relations will be severed and war will be declared on Japan. This is to demonstrate the spirit of our independent nation. It is not something that an independent country should do to merely hope that foreigners will uphold justice and only adopt a policy of calmness and endurance. We humbly request that you observe the national situation, comply with public opinion, rectify the army, and fight to the death on the battlefield to annihilate the Japanese invaders and restore our homeland. The spirit of the late Premier is what we rely on. We hereby telegraph this message, humbly requesting your consideration and implementation. We await your orders with sorrow and indignation. The Shanghai Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association's Citizens' Assembly.

Telegraph Requesting the Guangdong Faction to Abandon Previous Grievances To Mr. Sun Zhesheng, Gu Xiangqin, Wang Jingwei, Chen Bonan, Tang Shaochuan of Guangzhou: Japan is taking advantage of our country's preoccupation with disaster relief to disrupt East Asian peace and send troops to invade, occupying Liaoning and Jilin provinces and threatening Tianjin and Beijing. The pain of national subjugation is imminent. The Shanghai Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association, with the determination to resist Japan and save the country, convened an anti-Japanese national salvation citizens' assembly the day before yesterday and resolved that you, as great figures of the Party and the country, who created the Republic of China, have differences only due to political disagreements. At this time of national crisis, it is hoped that you will abandon previous grievances and resist Japan together with the Central Government to jointly defend against foreign aggression. The Shanghai Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association's Citizens' Assembly.

Declaration Issued by the Liaoning Fellow Association Yesterday 128

Executive Committee Meeting Convened This Morning

The Anti-Japanese Association of Northeastern Fellow Townsmen in Shanghai will convene the second Executive Committee meeting at 9:00 AM today at the Chinese YMCA on Sichuan Road to discuss all anti-Japanese work. Yesterday, it issued a declaration stating that "Now, on the land of Manchuria, the bloody blood of the slaughtered is being spread, and the earth-shattering artillery fire is continuing. The fierce and strong Japanese imperialists are using their sharp guns and cannons to massacre tens of millions of northeastern compatriots, carrying out their bestial plundering ambitions." "Compatriots of the whole country, small and weak nations of the world, as long as we are not cold-blooded, can we still restrain our surging anger and passion?" "Only the northeastern people are drowning in the deep waters of plundering and slaughter, but the military and political authorities continue to play their deceptive tricks of serenity, forbearance, and non-resistance, while the great powers have clearly shown their ugly face of helping the strong and oppressing the weak in their so-called 'League of Nations'." "At this time, can we still wait quietly for others? We, the people who have suffered directly, can only unite and rely on our own strength to make a desperate resistance as vanguards." "Therefore, in this national fever for unity against Japan, we, the fellow townsmen of all circles in Shanghai who have stayed in Shanghai, with the enthusiasm and determination of vanguard assaults, and after rapid preparation, produced the organization of the Anti-Japanese Association of Northeastern Fellow Townsmen in Shanghai on September 26." "At the meeting, each fellow townsman was eager to express their hatred for the atrocities and their grief for the suffering compatriots, and in an atmosphere of grief and indignation, many anti-Japanese plans were carefully decided." "We have long known that the Japanese slaves, harboring their ambitions of aggression, have provoked more than seventy times in the Northeast in recent years, and finally sent troops to the Northeast to begin their bloody massacre." "Corpses are piled up like mountains in Shenyang, tens of thousands of unemployed workers are waiting to die, and hundreds of thousands of refugees are fleeing outside the border every day." "This kind of atrocity, the Japanese imperialists still say is not a military occupation." "Compatriots, compatriots of the whole country, the blood of the past 'May 3rd' 'May 30th' and the recent 'Korean Incident' is still not cold, and now this even more tragic massacre has continued to arrive." "However, we also know that this time the Japanese slaves' atrocities are not a simple fact, but have a serious economic, political and military background." "In order to achieve the ambition of swallowing Manchuria and Mongolia, in order to expel the economic power of the United States in Manchuria, in order to attack the Soviet Union in North Manchuria, which is in absolute conflict with it, in order to stabilize its domestic economic panic, and in order to alleviate the anti-Japanese sentiment in Korea, it is forced to start this blatant plundering and cruel massacre." "However, we know even more that under these complicated and intricate conflicts and contradictions, although imperialism uses all kinds of tactics of plundering and slaughter, its impending collapse is still inevitable and unavoidable." "Violent Japan, as well as other imperialists, must completely collapse under the unity of the oppressed masses."

Shanghai County Anti-Japanese Movement Propaganda Week 129

Mass Meeting Held in Tangwan

The Shanghai County Party Headquarters, in light of the recent violent occupation of the Northeast Provinces by Japan, and in order to intensify anti-Japanese efforts, has expanded the Anti-Japanese Aid to Overseas Chinese Association into the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association. After the second joint meeting of the Executive and Supervisory Committees, it was decided that from September 28th to October 5th would be Anti-Japanese Movement Propaganda Week, during which mass meetings would be held in various districts in turn. The day before yesterday was the first day of Propaganda Week, held at the Tangwan Town public sports ground in the second district. Despite the torrential rain, the participation of the masses was extremely enthusiastic. The details of the meeting are summarized below:

Attendance: Peng Liren, Standing Committee Member of the County Party Headquarters; Jin Zuobin, of the Mass Education Center; all party members from the second district; people from all walks of life; students from various schools; Boy Scouts; and representatives from various groups, totaling approximately several thousand people.

Departure for Propaganda: The meeting passed several important motions, and after passing an important telegram, the attendees set out for propaganda despite the rain, dispersing around 6 PM.

Important Telegram: The telegram to Commander-in-Chief Chiang read: "The violent Japanese have invaded our territory, massacred our people, and lost thousands of miles of land. More than ten days have passed, and we have not seen the central government issue an order for mobilization, sever diplomatic relations, or declare war. We only hear of appeals for aid to the League of Nations and empty protests. We do not know that international justice has long perished. With enemy troops penetrating deep into the interior, you still want to negotiate through protests. Is this not an unprecedented absurdity? We earnestly request Commander-in-Chief Chiang to personally lead a large army to the Northeast to fight against Japan. The entire district's people pledge to be your support. All rear party and government problems, eliminate the boundaries between Beijing and Guangdong, and let advanced figures within the party cooperate to govern. Armed comrades, except for a reasonable number left to suppress bandits, should all go to the front to fight, boost morale, and jointly save the nation from peril. This is the only chance. If you continue to be keen on internal strife and procrastinate, I fear that the Song people's debates will be unsettled, and the Jin troops will have already crossed the river. The chief culprit of national subjugation will be our authorities who cannot evade blame. We present our urgent words with utmost anxiety and await orders." (Omitted below.) The telegram to the Central Party Headquarters read: "Japan has sent troops without cause, invading our Northeast provinces. The officials guarding the territory have retreated at every turn. In a matter of days, thousands of miles of land have been lost. Countless lives and property have been lost. This is the greatest shame and humiliation. Hope for mediation by the League of Nations has been dashed. Asking for help from others is not as good as striving for ourselves. Moreover, Red Russia is gathering troops on the border, eager to try. Once contact is made, our country's territory will immediately become a world battlefield, the people will be devastated, and tombs will become ruins. Thinking of the future, we cannot help but tremble. We earnestly request the central government to swiftly dispatch a large army to the Northeast to drive the Japanese troops out of our territory, protect our country's territory, and save our country's people. World peace can also rely on this for maintenance. Please do not procrastinate and lose the opportunity." (Omitted below.)

The Two-Road Party Headquarters immediately organized an anti-Japanese national salvation propaganda train team, departing at 5 AM today to conduct propaganda along the train, carrying various propaganda materials to raise the public's deep awareness and unite against Japan. The telegrams are recorded separately below.

Telegram to International Organizations: Urgent, to the World Association of Young Women's Christian Associations, the International Council of Women, the International Women's League for Peace and Freedom, the International Women's Temperance Union, and the International Women's Suffrage Alliance: At a time when the world is experiencing economic panic, and countries are too preoccupied to care for others, and when China is suffering from floods and is unable to resist, Japan, taking advantage of the Nakamura Incident, is carrying out military aggression, destroying railways privately, and brazenly dispatching troops to occupy Shenyang, Changchun, Yingkou, Andong, Liaoyang, and other places; burning our barracks, arsenals, government offices, and civilian houses; detaining our important officials; disarming our military police; capturing our large guard detachments; and massacring our innocent civilians, discarding humanity, violating the spirit of the Washington Conference, and violating the provisions of the Kellogg-Briand Pact, directly destroying peace in East Asia and indirectly endangering world peace. In the past three days, the situation has worsened, with troops being deployed and generals sent, steadily advancing. Jilin has also been seized, and Beijing and Tianjin are also reported to be strained. Japanese warships along the coast are landing to demonstrate. It is unknown when this kind of ambition and brutality will end. Today, Japan's barbarity and cruelty are a hundred times greater than the Jinan Massacre of that year, and the public's indignation is also incomparable to the past. However, the Japanese side is accustomed to one-sided propaganda and will easily confuse international audiences. Therefore, we present the course of events to clarify the responsibility of the aggressor. We hope that you will weigh the facts, make a fair judgment based on reason, uphold justice, safeguard fairness, arouse the sympathy of Europeans and Americans, create a strong public opinion, and adopt an attitude of supporting the weak and suppressing the strong to stop the Japanese military's brutal actions. If so, China will be fortunate, and the world will be fortunate. We hope you will consider this and await your guidance.

Telegram to Japan: Furthermore, a telegram was sent to the Japan Women's Temperance Union, saying: Your country has dispatched troops to Manchuria and Mongolia without any reason, without any prior warning of a declaration of war, which is a clear violation of the Kellogg-Briand Pact and a disruption of world peace. We ask your union comrades to unanimously urge your government to withdraw its troops to their original places immediately and to avoid the occurrence of such atrocities forever, which is what we hope for.

International Replies: The International Women's League for Peace and Freedom replied in a telegram yesterday, saying: We have just received your telegram and express our sympathy. We will immediately show the original telegram to the Japanese representative stationed in Geneva, urging them to send a telegram to their home government to stop the atrocities immediately. At the same time, all members of our committee will do their best to advocate public opinion in Geneva and express our deepest sympathy to your country. Furthermore, the National Women's Suffrage Alliance replied in a telegram yesterday, saying: We have read your telegram and are deeply shocked. The 400,000 suffragist women around the world pay close attention to world peace. Since your association has reported the truth of this matter to our association, our association will definitely report the truth to the League of Nations and do our best to find a solution.

Municipal Citizens' Association for the Promotion of National Goods 133

Emergency Meeting of Members Held Yesterday

The Shanghai Municipal Citizens' Association for the Promotion of National Goods convened an emergency meeting of all factory members at 3 PM yesterday to discuss anti-Japanese national salvation work. 128 people attended, and Chen Yiting, Shen Shuyu, and Chen Binghui were elected as the presidium. After formal greetings, Chairman Chen reported the purpose of the meeting and the situation of the Japanese military invasion. Xu Yunhui, Liu Zhongying, Chen Nansun, Zhang Deqi, Zhang Qingfa, Yang Yucheng, and Xu Jianruo, and other representatives successively expressed their opinions, with many words of grief. The chairman summarized the public opinion and decided on the following: (1) Issue a solemn declaration; (2) Petition the central Guangdong governments to comply with public opinion and stop the war; (3) Request the government to concentrate its forces and declare war on Japan; (4) Severely punish those who lost national territory to warn against the future and appease public anger; (5) Advise the national people to actively boycott Japanese goods and promote national goods; (6) Strive to manufacture national defense military supplies; (7) National goods factories voluntarily decide not to import Japanese raw materials; (8) National goods factories jointly establish a raw materials factory; (9) Send letters to various factories, prohibiting raising the selling price of products; (10) Organize a team to promote the use of national goods; (11) Request the Municipal Chamber of Commerce to advise various shops to display national goods samples in their shop windows; (12) Establish a national goods tea party to concentrate production and sales forces; (13) Send letters to the Entertainment Association, asking them to send letters to all performers to participate in anti-Japanese national salvation and promotion of national goods materials during performances; (14) Send letters to various institutions, organizations, and leaders from all walks of life, leading the oath to promote national goods, etc. The attending representatives first took the oath to promote these measures. The oath reads: "I solemnly pledge to adhere to the legacy of the late Prime Minister Sun Yat-sen and promote national goods for the country. I vow never to use foreign goods for the rest of my life, promote national goods, and take on the responsibility of advising relatives and friends to use national goods in order to fulfill my national duty and save the country from disaster. If I violate this oath, I will be subject to the most severe condemnation of conscience. I solemnly swear, on this day, month, and year of the Republic of China, the person taking the oath, the witness." The oath has been printed and will be distributed widely soon to achieve significant results.

City Merchants Enthusiastically Support the Boy Scouts' Resistance Against Japan The City Merchants' Boy Scout Troop (the 50th Troop of the Boy Scouts of China) announced the merchants' inherent duty to resist Japan and save the nation, and that Boy Scout training is the most practical training. Since then, merchants in the city have been flocking to the troop to request copies of the regulations. The troop stated that this autumn is the time for the third recruitment of new members. Due to the national crisis, to allow Shanghai merchants to participate in training as much as possible in order to serve the country, a plan to expand the organization and broadly recruit members has been drafted and submitted to the City Merchants' Association for adoption. It is also heard that the troop's "Instructions for Joining" have been completely exhausted. Once the recruitment is completed, another method will be announced and notified again.

The Third Brigade of the Defense Corps Intensifies its Work The Third Brigade of the Shanghai Hubei District Defense Corps issued an emergency notice yesterday, ordering all members to intensify drills and training. On the same day, a public notice was posted, stating that a considerable number of obligated members who have served for three years are about to transfer to the reserve team, and it is urgent to continue recruiting new members to fill the vacancies. Anyone who is over 20 and under 35 years old, and has a legitimate occupation, regardless of province, may go to the brigade headquarters at the entrance of Baoshan Road, Baoshan Lane, Zhabei, from 8:00 AM to 11:00 AM and from 2:00 PM to 5:00 PM every day to register.

All Employees of the Wuzhou Gu Ben Factory are Fully Armed Mr. Xiang Songmao, the general manager of Wuzhou Gu Ben Soap and Pharmaceutical Factory, yesterday organized all employees of the factory into a volunteer army battalion. Except for employees over 50 years old who are old and weak and cannot undergo training, all men and women have joined. Now, Ruan Xiaojun, a military instructor from Jiaotong University, has been hired to provide one hour of strict training from 5:00 PM to 6:00 PM every day in preparation for declaring war on Japan. The position of battalion commander will be concurrently held by the general manager of the factory, and other company and platoon leaders will be concurrently held by important employees of the factory.

Resolutions of the Baolong Hospital Nurses The nurses of Baolong Hospital are extremely indignant at the brutal actions of the violent Japanese. On the 27th, more than 80 male and female nurses were called together to organize a national salvation association to resist Japan, which has now been formally established. Resolutions: (1) Send representatives to major hospital nurses' associations and medical and pharmaceutical institutions in the city to publicize and unite to expand the group and cooperate. (2) All preparations for departure to the battlefield for military first aid. (3) Request the hospital to stop purchasing Japanese pharmaceutical materials. Working all night for several days, the situation is very tense.

Declaration of the Electrical Experiment Research Association The Chinese Electrical Experiment Research Association issued a declaration yesterday regarding the Japanese atrocities, stating: (the beginning omitted) Now that the disaster of national subjugation is imminent and the national situation is in danger, all of our compatriots across the country must rise up in unison to urge the government to cease internal strife and resist foreign aggression, vowing to fight the Japanese pirates to the death. It is better to be shattered jade than to be a whole tile, to fight desperately with our backs to the city, or to annihilate those villains. Preparing for battle and killing enemies is the only way to protect our country. We, as members of this association, are merely subjects of the nation, and dare not fail to exert our utmost to be at the forefront, going through fire and water. We will not hesitate to dedicate our blood and break our necks. Writing this in indignation, blood and tears together, we hereby declare.

Review of Japanese Goods by the Electrical Silk Weaving Industry On the afternoon of the 27th, the Electrical Silk Weaving Industry convened a joint meeting of relevant industries to review Japanese goods. Wang Shiqiang presided over the meeting. Matters for discussion: (1) Regarding the issue of textile raw materials, it was resolved that domestic goods should be used first for the fine yarn of the weaving machine. If it is insufficient, the Great China Company on Wuma Road, Mr. Qian Xuanqing, or the Changshenghua firm on Sichuan Road, Mr. Chen Liqing, may be entrusted to contact British factories to handle fine yarn. (2) Regarding the issue of mechanical material items, it was resolved that He Dehuai and Xie Liangcai of the Mechanical Material Industry Association would be responsible for notifying that domestic goods should be used as a priority. If no domestic goods are available as substitutes, European and American goods may be substituted. In the future, if anyone still uses Japanese goods as substitutes, they will be handed over to the Anti-Japanese Association for punishment. (3) Regarding the issue of processing business, it was resolved that all dyeing and refining of goods by electrical silk weaving factories in the city must be sent to refining factories established by Chinese people, and no longer seek dyeing and refining from Japanese people. The refining industry in the city should also be warned that the raw materials used should not still rely on Japanese goods, and substitutes must be sought urgently to show thoroughness. (4) Regarding mechanical matters, only Zhuyatie Iron Factory attended the meeting, and Mr. Xu Xuechang represented the report. The peach wood used on the machines manufactured by the factory has long been replaced by German goods, and magnetic parts and other parts will be replaced by domestic goods immediately. The resolution to be discussed should be implemented. There are still many other issues, all of which are thorough measures to resist Japanese goods and revitalize domestic products. The meeting ended as the jade rabbit was about to rise.

The Cotton Cloth Association Notifies the Sealing of Japanese Goods The Cotton Cloth Industry Association, after a resolution by the general assembly, reorganized the Special Committee on Japan into the Cotton Cloth Industry Anti-Japanese Committee, adding 20 inspectors to go to Mitsubishi Warehouse, Huishan and other piers every day to implement inspections. The third Anti-Japanese Committee also resolved that all Japanese goods owned by the industry should be sealed up from now on and not be bought or sold. Japanese goods ordered from foreign firms should also be returned in full immediately to show determination. The case has been recorded and notified to all members for compliance yesterday.

The Women's Association for the Promotion of Domestic Goods Restrains Stores from Selling Japanese Goods The Shanghai Women's Association for the Promotion of Domestic Goods held its eighth joint meeting of the executive and supervisory committees at the City Government Public Service Club at 4:00 PM yesterday. More than ten people attended, including Ma Yuying, Tang Guanyu, Zhou Jun, Chen Hongru, Ge Jinghe, Zheng Huichen, Chen Jingrong, Ding Shujing (represented by Zhang Peizhen), Wang Xiaoying (represented by Lin Kecong), and Lin Kecong. The Anti-Japanese Association Inspects Postal Packages The Anti-Japanese Association decided on the implementation method for inspecting Ningbo packages: 1. Negotiate with the post office to have the association send personnel to be stationed to inspect Japanese goods in postal packages. 2. Send a letter to the Chinese officials of the customs to pay attention to Japanese goods in postal packages. Once discovered, immediately notify or imply to the association's resident inspector. 3. The association will send a car to be stationed in the post office courtyard for the purpose of transporting detained postal packages. 4. The reconnaissance department will immediately investigate the activities of Japanese goods postal package brokers and provide a list to the standing committee for review. 5. A written warning will be issued to the brokers. If they still do not restrain themselves after one warning, the association should immediately follow the resolution of the All Circles Representative Congress and punish them.

Student Petition Group Returns to Shanghai 136

Arriving This Morning

In the past two days, the student petition groups from various universities in Shanghai who went to Beijing totaled about 3,600 people. Yesterday, they went to the National Government again to petition. The points they raised have been accepted by the National Government, and Chairman Chiang gave a public speech. The representatives were satisfied and left Beijing last night to return to Shanghai. Three temporary trains were prepared at Xiaguan Station and departed at 8:00 PM, 10:00 PM, and 11:30 PM, respectively. They are expected to arrive in Shanghai around 8:00 AM this morning. However, more than 400 students from Daxia University took the night train to Beijing again last night. Although the director of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, the director of the Education Bureau, and the railway authorities explained to them that the petition group that had gone to Beijing was already returning to Shanghai, and persuaded them to stop and avoid further travel, it was to no avail. The students still refused to get off the train, so the train left for Beijing.

Important News from the Anti-Japanese Aviation Industry 137

Liaoning Refugees Continue to Arrive After the fall of Liaoning, residents and merchants could not bear the abuse and slaughter by Japanese soldiers and fled one after another. The first batch of southerners who arrived in Shanghai via the sea route landed in Shanghai on the 25th, totaling more than 110 people. The second batch escaped from Shenyang, first arrived in Dalian Bay, and then took a ship to Shanghai, arriving yesterday with a total of 176 people. Women accounted for five-tenths, children accounted for two-tenths, and the rest were men. Most of them were families. After the Japanese soldiers entered Shenyang, they abandoned all their belongings and fled with their families. Among the refugees in the second batch yesterday, 33 were from Jiangsu, 31 were from Zhejiang, 11 were from Ningbo, 41 were from Shanghai, and 42 were from Fengtian who fled to Shanghai. In addition, there were refugees from Jiangxi, Guangdong, Henan, and other provinces, most of whom were merchants. The refugees from Jiangsu and Zhejiang were mostly women. When the refugees landed at the Huangpu Pier, they were all in a very embarrassed state. When the refugees left Fengtian, they fled in a hurry. They could not carry the clothes and property they had in Fengtian and had to prepare some travel expenses to leave as soon as possible. The losses were incalculable. Some even lacked clothes and shoes, which shows the urgency of their escape. According to a Zhejiang man named Yang among the refugees, after the Japanese soldiers forcibly occupied various agencies in Shenyang, they posted notices prohibiting non-Japanese people from entering. They also set up ambushes everywhere in the streets and roads, posing with their weapons as if they were about to shoot. Chinese people who were unaware and mistakenly passed through their scattered troops were often shot and killed. The Japanese soldiers killed a Chinese person as if they were killing a chicken or a dog. In this recent group of refugees from the south, many family members were shot and killed by Japanese soldiers for no reason, and their bodies could not be found. We have worked hard for thousands of miles to make a living and do business, but suddenly our families were destroyed, and we suffered the tragedy of being arbitrarily killed by foreign soldiers. Decades of hard work were destroyed in an instant. The country has troops, and the people pay taxes, but they cannot provide the slightest protection in times of danger. Moreover, they issued an order not to resist, which is clearly a willingness to be slaughtered. As the people of the eastern provinces, it is better to be a slave of a conquered country. When Mr. Yang spoke, he was in tears, and it was unbearable to listen. Except for those who had relatives and friends, the rest were temporarily staying in small inns, waiting to return to their original hometowns in the coming days. It is said that a third batch of refugees will arrive tomorrow.

Shanghai-Hong Kong Japanese Ships Suspend Operations As Japan Seizes the Eastern Provinces, which Affects the Survival of Our Nation, People Everywhere Have United to Resist. Chinese Merchants in Hong Kong Have Also Agreed to Sever Economic Relations with Japan, Stop Handling Japanese Goods, and Refuse to Take Japanese Ships. Now, They Have Taken a Step Further. All Dockworkers of Japanese Merchants Have Contacted Tugboat Gang Workers and Implemented a Strike. When Japanese Ships Arrive in Port, They Unanimously Refuse to Load and Unload Goods and Refuse to Carry Passengers. Their Solidarity is Even Stronger Than That of Shanghai Workers. The Japanese Can Do Nothing and Have Sent Telegrams to Shanghai, Ordering Shanghai Japanese Ships to Stop Carrying Goods and Passengers to Hong Kong. Yesterday, the Shanghai Nissin Company Received a Telegram and Ordered the Nanhua Liner Lushan Maru and Songshan Maru to Stop Going to Hong Kong and Sent Wireless Telegrams Notifying the Lushan Liner En Route to Proceed to Guangdong After Arriving in Shantou. From Today, Japanese Ships in Shanghai Will No Longer Carry Goods and Passengers to Hong Kong. The Business of the Hong Kong Liners of Jardine Matheson and Taikoo Docks is Booming.

Striking at Sino-Japanese Liners The effectiveness of this boycott is rarely seen in the past. Most of the transactions of various Japanese firms have completely stopped. Since the Anti-Japanese Association announced that if there are unscrupulous merchants privately transporting goods for the Japanese, they will be severely punished if found out, customs brokers and Japanese merchants have completely cut off contact. In the past, goods from the Sino-Japanese liners of the Japanese Postal Company were not boycotted. This time, such as the Rokko Maru, Aso Maru, Tsukuba Maru, and Kasagi Maru arriving in Shanghai, no goods were loaded, and exports were even less, only 10% of what they used to be. The Yangtze River liners of Nissin, in addition to slightly carrying Japanese sugar and kelp, have practically no other goods. Yesterday, the Osaka Changsha Maru left Shanghai for Tianjin, carrying only one ton of export goods. The business of the Dalian Steamship Company has also fallen by nine-tenths. The Shanghai Toyo Customs Broker has almost completely stopped and has nothing to do. Recently, various Japanese merchants in Shanghai are also anxious about this, fearing that if our country continues to persist, Japanese merchants will have no foothold in China.

Japanese Warships Sail to Wenzhou In recent days, Japanese warships have been coming to the Yangtze River one after another. There is already the first team in North China and the second team. There are also two from Lushun and Magong sailing to our country's seaports. Recently, the warship Tsushima has been transferred from Sasebo and loaded with marines to Shanghai. Yesterday, it was heard that it has been decided to land part of the army in Haideng, and the rest ordered the Tsushima to carry them to Nanjing in the coming days to demonstrate, and ordered the Hirado to sail to Hankou, transferred the Uji to Shanghai, and transferred three destroyers, the Yanagi, Aoi, and Take, from Magong to Wenzhou in a hurry. The Navy Ministry of the country has also organized the 25th warship team, sending eight destroyers, three gunboats, and one cruiser, preparing to order them to enter various parts of central China.

Silk Merchants from Andong Flee to Shanghai After the violent Japanese forcibly occupied Shenyang, Andong was also occupied. Andong is a large trading port with a thriving commercial market. The wild cocoon silk produced in the Northeast is distributed through Andong as a market. There are many wild silk factories in Andong. After the violent Japanese forcibly occupied Andong this time, the source of wild cocoon silk tended to stop. The wealthy merchants all took their families on foreign ships to seek refuge. Yesterday, the Taikoo Company's Zhoushan ship sailed from Andong to Shanghai, carrying the aforementioned gentlemen and merchants seeking refuge, totaling about fifty or sixty people, most of whom were silk merchants. They all stayed in various wild silk warehouses. Yesterday, I met Mr. Jin, a wild silk merchant who fled to Shanghai from Andong. He said that after the Japanese army invaded the Chinese streets of Andong and occupied various agencies, the shops automatically closed the next day, and the silk factories also stopped work. The price of banknotes fell tragically. The Japanese inconvertible gold notes (i.e., old man notes) were popular in Northeast China on weekdays, and each yuan could be exchanged for two yuan and six or seven corners. At this time, it fell sharply to two yuan. On the day we set off, each yuan could only be exchanged for one yuan and five corners. The financial panic reached its extreme. The wild cocoon silk inventory is limited, but various places are preparing to raise silkworms (i.e., wild silkworms) and release seeds. Many people are fleeing. This blow will definitely cause a reduction in the harvest of silkworms in the future.

Special Curfew in the Gaochang Temple Area 139

The Gaochang Temple area of this city is a key military location, containing important institutions such as an arsenal, naval fleet headquarters, shipyard, aircraft factory, and steel mill. With Sino-Japanese negotiations now urgent, a special curfew has been implemented every night starting yesterday after 8:00 PM. Without a password or pass, no one can freely enter or exit the factories. The defense is jointly maintained by the arsenal's guards and the naval guard battalion. It will return to normal at 6:00 AM.

Shanghai-Chongqing Air Service Now Being Prepared

Because the stations along the Shanghai-Yichang line of the China National Aviation Corporation were flooded and are now free of standing water, the company resumed service on the Shanghai-Yichang line yesterday morning at 7:00 AM, carrying mail and passengers. Stops are made at all stations along the line as usual. It is also reported that the company is actively preparing for the Shanghai-Chongqing air service, with the aim of realizing it in the shortest possible time.

The King and Queen of Siam went to the United States in April to treat an eye ailment. They have now recovered and are returning home on the Canadian Empress. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs is also not preparing to receive them due to the ongoing national crisis.

News from Various Provinces Regarding Disaster Relief Yesterday 143

News from the Jiangsu Flood Relief Association

The Tragedy of Xinghua's Flood Disaster: The flood disaster in Xinghua is extremely serious. Recently, the Xinghua Chamber of Commerce's temporary flood relief group sent a report on the flood disaster in Xinghua County. Every word is filled with grief and brings tears to the eyes. The original text is as follows: "Heaven has punished our Xinghua, turning it into a watery realm. The disaster affects the entire county, something never heard of before. Since the breach of the You-Shao Canal embankment, our people, hundreds of thousands of them, thought they would all perish together. Now, they are still eking out an existence, but we do not know how they will survive. Our association, its spirit just settling,勉盡未死之責、不爲死者呼寃但爲生者乞命敢將最近調查所得災狀及臨時救濟辦法報告如下、(I) Losses of life: Telegraph communications have been cut off since the day the Yun embankment breached. Two-丈 high torrents rushed down, and hurricane-force rain fell non-stop all night. People, as if in a dream, suspected that the water was falling from the sky and fled in panic, not knowing where to go. Hiding in small boats was considered the best option, but who knew that the waves would surge and capsize in an instant? Seeking life turned into seeking death. Those who did not have time to flee clung to the water, shouting for help, climbing trees and roofs, hoping to survive. But the trees broke, and the roofs collapsed, and they were still swallowed up by the boundless waters. Corpses floated everywhere, but there was no one to rescue them and no place to bury them. Now that the water has subsided slightly, people still hear about those who are lost due to the wind and danger every day. It is estimated that the total number of deaths in the county is more than the number of wretched ghosts under the breached dikes of You and Shao. If the water level can return to normal in the future, an accurate number can be obtained by checking the household registers. (II) Losses of food: Xingyi has suffered two great harvests and one major disaster in the last three years. Food was already extremely scarce, but this year's opening of the dams led to even more destruction. The usual practice of opening the Cheluo dam seven days before autumn was followed by the consecutive opening of the Xin and Nan dams, causing the green crops in the fields to be almost completely submerged. Fortunately, the eastern part of the county still has Yongfeng, Heta, Lao Zhong, Xia Wang, and Da Jiong, which were not breached, and a small harvest can be obtained, which is of some help. But the 800-丈 breach in the Yun embankment caused the water to rise rapidly and rush down. The various forts were unable to resist and collapsed one after another. In a few days, the small amount of rice harvested earlier was lost again. A current survey shows that only those who have more grain-producing land in the area can temporarily survive. Those who have less land or no land account for two-thirds of the county's population and are waiting to be fed, unable to wait any longer. (III) Losses of housing: After the opening of the three dams in Xingyi, the entire city fell into the abyss of the Nine Springs. The water depth in high houses is three to four feet, and low houses are submerged to the eaves, or even completely submerged. Residents in the water are constantly in danger of capsizing. But two hurricanes and rainstorms came one after another. The wind increased the power of the water, and the water rode the wind, with the waves reaching the tops of the trees and the city walls were pierced in fourteen places. Temples near the water around the city, such as Banruo Temple, Guanyin Pavilion, Jile Temple, Dizang Temple, and Longzhu Temple, famous monasteries, were either completely destroyed or partially collapsed. Other public and private houses had collapsed walls and cannot be counted. The most tragic thing is Zhongbao Village, a major town north of the city, which is surrounded by a large lake. More than 1,000 households in the town have only eleven houses left standing. Even the tall houses in the town could not avoid being washed away. Who can guarantee the existence of the other thatched houses in the countryside? Visiting the countryside, all one sees are ruined buildings and collapsed walls. Everything in the houses has been washed away. The disaster victims are huddled in small boats or perched on broken roofs. They encounter wind and rain, and wild cries are heard everywhere. The future is bleak, and they do not know when they will be able to settle down. (IV) Other losses: The Huai River has been flowing east for more than a month, and it is not known when it will recede. Recalling the breach of the Qingshui Pool in the fifth year of Tongzhi and the overflowing embankment of the Grand Canal in the tenth year of the Republic, the flood was not as great as this, and the storage period was not as long. Regarding agricultural matters, such as windmills being almost completely destroyed, and cattle being sold cheaply, people have no livelihood for a long time and no place to live. The misery is beyond description. In addition, schools have been forced to close, and students have also become refugees and lost their places. Crafts have been abandoned, and workers have no way to beg. And in our business community, goods have been damaged and capital has been lost. Those who cannot resume business are also numerous. The four classes of people have suffered the same disaster, equal to annihilation. This was not something that could have been anticipated when the dams were opened. Now, because the damage is so great and the pain is so deep, all government affairs have been abandoned. It is extremely difficult to maintain the precarious situation. After the meeting, feeling sad, we were deeply concerned that order would not be maintained. After opening the dams, we first籌　平市米局 to stabilize people's hearts. Later, we also joined with the local government to organize relief groups to 　　 rescue from all sides. Thanks to the provincial government officials, we received a large amount of funds for emergency relief, and we also承江南北慈善大家、分别合組救災會、救災團、先後　興施放振糧振品、仍予收容難民, we have already rescued more than 5,000 people. Deep benevolence and great kindness, we celebrate our rebirth. However, the disaster is widespread and there are many people in need of rescue, and the dangerous period has not yet been overcome. We still懇各當道各慈善界, we are guided by the principle of rescuing people and rescuing thoroughly, and we are making large-scale plans and long-term assistance. Members come to Xing and督同地方, we will carry out universal relief. The disaster victims will be spared death, and we will be grateful. Fonian, there are many disasters everywhere and great difficulties in the days to come. Recently, members of the association have gathered and decided to form a temporary flood relief group. In addition to the overall local relief, we will specifically筹办平糶麵粉两月, continue to办减价粥局三月,兼施篷蓆,并给寒衣, the funds needed are estimated to be 100,000 yuan. All industries will raise as much as possible within their capabilities, and we will also叩各大商埠善之士, give assistance to make up for local deficiencies and謀秩序之苟安, we only seek to度到來春, and then make续救办法, however, this 屬治標之策, it only济燃眉, as for its fundamental remedy, we should恳水利當道, quickly将运堤决口之二十七处, and the date of completion is 尅期完堵, in order to block its source, and the disaster will be restored, so there is hope, otherwise, the upstream Honghu Lake will move to Xingyi, and the disaster of vicissitudes of life will not be in the present, but in the coming year, what people's livelihood can be said to be, the Xinghua County Chamber of Commerce temporary flood relief group is respectful."

The Enthusiasm for Contributing to Disaster Relief: Since its establishment, the association has raised funds from all over the world. People from all walks of life are in great pain. Both north and south of the Yangtze River are deeply affected by the flood, and the breaches of Gao and Shao dikes have turned the five villages under Yangzhou into swamps. They are all reducing their clothing and food and donating money to help with disaster relief. The education sector is also collecting funds and donating. Teachers and staff of Nanjing Middle School Experimental Elementary School, in addition to contributing their own money, are also saving public banquet expenses to help disaster relief. Elementary school students are also saving money from snacks to help disaster relief. Even school workers in the school who earn only a few yuan a month are donating generously, such as Huang Gui, Liu Gui, Wang Pei, Wan He, Xia Lin, Ren Er, Wang Cheng, Yuan Cheng, Liu Cheng, and Chen Ma, all of whom have made donations. This shows that people are eager to help the public and that everyone has the same heart.

Letter Requesting Curb on Rising Prices of Chinese Yarn 144

Zhang Zilian of the Samsung Cotton Weaving Factory sent a letter yesterday to the Shanghai National Products Factory Federation, stating that Japan is forcibly occupying our Northeast, and the people of the whole country are vowing to implement a thorough boycott of Japanese goods with all effective means. Unexpectedly, a few unscrupulous merchants are taking advantage of the opportunity to raise the prices of domestic yarn and other raw materials. Their conscienceless and insane actions are not enough to quell public anger even if they were to be skinned alive. Please, in accordance with the purpose of resisting Japan and saving the country, take swift action. For example, 16-count yarn should not exceed 160 taels, and 20-count yarn should not exceed 170 taels. Otherwise, let the prices rise, and not only will small-scale industrial and commercial enterprises not be able to unite in the cause of resisting Japan and saving the country due to the high cost of raw materials.

Song Shiyi Succeeds as Director of the Arsenal 145

New Appointee Takes Office Tomorrow

The Labor Union Still Retains Mr. Guo

Mr. Guo Chengen, director of the Shanghai Arsenal, has found his duties overwhelming since simultaneously serving as director of the Two Roads Bureau. He has submitted his resignation to the Ministry of Military Administration, which has been approved. Mr. Song Shiyi has been appointed as the new director of the arsenal. The details are as follows:

Resignation Process: Since Guo Chengen, director of the Shanghai 　　　　　　　　　, also serves as director of the Two Roads Bureau, the duties of the Roads Bureau are busy, 　　 and there are duties as director of the Arsenal, so the chief of the general affairs department of the factory, Xu Mujun, was appointed to act as the agent. The factory machinery was once accidentally失愼, 赵数日, the gun factory also reported a fire. Although Guo tried his best to investigate, he has not yet found out the truth. In addition, Guo holds two positions, which inevitably leads to顾此失彼, so he submitted his resignation to the Ministry of Military Administration the day before yesterday.

Succession Already Determined: After the Ministry of Military Administration received Guo's resignation, they understood that Guo had difficulties. The affairs of the arsenal are extremely important and should be handled by a specialist who is responsible at the factory every day. Therefore, Chen Gongxia, the political vice minister and director of the Ordnance Department of the ministry, immediately approved the resignation and appointed Song Shiyi, the deputy director of the department, to succeed him. After Song received the appointment, he has decided to come to Shanghai tomorrow to take office.

Supervision of Handover: In addition to ordering Song to take over, the Ministry of Military Administration also instructed Du Zhiying, director of the Accounting Department of the Military Needs Department of the Ministry, and others to come to Shanghai to supervise the handover. The original order stated, "In order to comply with the order, Guo Chengen, director of the Shanghai Arsenal of the Ministry, has been approved to resign, and Song Shiyi has been appointed to fill the vacancy, and orders have been issued separately. Now, Du Zhiying, director of the Accounting Section of the Military Needs Department, and Zhuang Quan, a special commissioner of the Ordnance Department, are dispatched to the factory to supervise the handover. In addition to the separate announcement, this order is hereby issued for compliance."

Guo Jinjing: After the Ministry of Military Administration approved Guo's resignation, Guo immediately sent a telegram to the new director, Song Shiyi, at around 3:00 PM yesterday, asking him to come to Shanghai to take office as soon as possible. Because he was奉蔣主席之召, he took the night express train to Jinjing last night.

Resignation of Staff: After Guo's resignation was approved, Xu Mujun, chief of the general affairs department of the factory, Zhang Deqing, chief of the engineering department, Li Jingxia, chief of the accounting section, Ding Houfu, chief of the auditing section, Xie Jizu, chief of the purchasing section, and Zhou Daifu, chief of the general affairs section, have all resigned one after another.

Song's Brief Biography: The new director, Song Shiyi, is 46 years old and from Hunan. He graduated from the Japanese Army Officer Academy and served as an army regimental commander and brigade commander. He is currently the deputy director of the Ordnance Department of the Ministry of Military Administration and is well-versed in military administration and academics.

Trade Union Retains: Guo Chengen, director of the Shanghai Arsenal, resigned from the position of director of the Shanghai Arsenal to the Military Industry Department of the Ministry of Military Administration because of his heavy duties. He has been granted approval by the authorities. However, the Trade Union learned of the situation and was deeply saddened. Since Guo came to the factory, he has spared no effort in rectifying and planning and has been thinking of ways to increase wages to alleviate the hardships of the workers. Therefore, the workers unanimously support him and work hard to produce products. Therefore, the association earnestly retains Guo in accordance with the wishes of the workers and telegraphed the director of the Ordnance Department yesterday to retain Guo's tenure. Contracts Previously Signed by the Labor Union 148

Party and Government Agencies to Review

The Shanghai Executive Committee believes that the Shanghai Labor Union was previously abolished by a clear order from the Central Government, and the labor-management contracts it signed with the capital will be reviewed by party and government agencies to determine whether to retain or abolish them in order to benefit the workers. The following is a letter from the Municipal Party Headquarters to the Social Affairs Bureau: "Dear Sirs, the Municipal Labor Union was previously abolished by a clear order from the Central Government. However, the Labor Union and others have signed many labor-management contracts with the capital. The contracts should not be cancelled along with the Labor Union's loss of corporate status, resulting in the sudden loss of protection for the majority of workers. In view of this, the Central Government has stipulated that the local party and government agencies should review the contracts in accordance with the current laws and regulations in order to separately retain or abolish them to benefit the workers and the real economy. This has been decided by the ninth regular meeting of our association, and Hou Dachun, Lu Jingshi, Huang Zaoxiong, Yang Qingyuan, and Zhou Sizhi have been designated to work with your bureau to send personnel to review the contracts. We hereby send this letter to you for your reference and reply."

The Case of Yin Wenlong's Tragic Death in a Plane Crash 150

His Wife Sues for Compensation

Judgment Rejected Yesterday

Yin Wenlong, a comprador of the Anli foreign firm in Hankou, took the Shanghai Airlines Shanghai plane to Hankou on December 9th last year. However, the plane collided with a ship's mast in the Huangpu River, and the plane crashed. The pilot and passengers were injured, and Yin died of serious injuries. His wife, Sun Yuefang, argued that since her deceased husband did not sign the passenger ticket he purchased, the rules printed on the ticket could not be binding. She hired a lawyer and sued the airline in accordance with Article 　　　 of the Civil Law　　　 , Section 3 of the District Court, requesting that the airline be held liable and compensate for funeral expenses, orphan education expenses, consolation money, and loss money, totaling more than 100,000 yuan. The case has been tried and the final judgment was awaited. Yesterday morning was the date for the judgment of the case. Lawyers from both sides were in court waiting for instructions. The presiding judge, Li Mo, took his seat and announced the verdict. The main text of the verdict stated, "The plaintiff's lawsuit is rejected, and the litigation costs shall be borne by the plaintiff."

City Social Affairs Bureau Burns Rice Borer Eggs and Moths 151

680,532 Rice Borer Eggs

167,402 Rice Borers

—Removing One Rice Borer Egg Mass Can Increase Grain Yield by Half a Catty—

Recently, rice borers have caused damage, resulting in poor autumn harvests and significant harm to people's food supply. The Municipal Social Affairs Bureau has repeatedly organized cooperative rice borer eradication experimental zones and offered subsidies to farmers who specifically contract to participate. This includes activities such as using lights to attract moths and removing egg masses to eliminate rice borers. At the same time, personnel were dispatched to various districts, carrying slogans, illustrations, and rice borer eradication tools, to explain methods of capture. Furthermore, municipal committee members from each district were ordered to supervise local farmers to work together in preventing and eliminating the pests to avoid crop damage. However, farmers in various districts mostly looked on, and capturing the pests was not actively pursued. If this continues without attention, the consequences are unimaginable. In order to motivate farmers to actively search for and capture rice borer eggs and moths, the bureau formulated purchasing methods and weekly report forms, which were submitted to the Municipal Government for approval. Initially, 2,000 yuan was allocated for pest eradication expenses. From July 1st to August 30th, a total of 680,532 egg masses and 167,402 rice borers were collected. The total expenditure for the purchases was 1,077 yuan, 3 jiao, 1 fen, and 3 li. The bureau transported all the collected materials to an open space in front of the Xiejiao Flower God Temple yesterday afternoon at 2 pm for burning. Representatives from the Municipal Party Headquarters and the Municipal Government were sent to supervise. Municipal committee members from various districts and bureau staff were present to observe. It was found that the rice borer eggs and moths purchased had a significant impact on increasing the rice grain harvest in the city. Removing one rice borer egg mass can reduce over a hundred rice stalk; with each stalk yielding an estimated 150 grains, removing one rice borer egg mass can increase grain yield by half a catty. Based on the 680,532 egg masses collected, the city can increase its harvest by over 340,000 catties, equivalent to over 340,000 dan or over 1,700 shi of polished rice. The increased yield from purchasing rice borers is not included in this calculation. The cost is small, but the returns are substantial. A summary of the purchase of rice borer moths and eggs in various districts of the city is shown in the following table:

Summary of Rice Borer Moth and Egg Purchases in Shanghai Districts

District | Rice Borer Eggs | Rice Borers | Purchase Amount (Yuan) | Actual Purchase Days | Purchase Days | Start Date | End Date | Remarks

------- | -------- | -------- | -------- | -------- | -------- | -------- | -------- | --------

| | | | | | | |

YinHang | 258,952 | 132,534 | 1005.08 | 3 | 2 | July 8 | August 30 | The institute increased the price once and reduced it twice

Caojing | 34,080 | 33,868 | 179.613 | 4 | 0 | July 1 | August 12 | The institute increased the price once

Agricultural Experiment Field | 387,500 | 592,62 | 3 | 3 | July 14 | August 31 | The institute reduced the price once

Total | 680,532 | 167,402 | 1777.313 | | | | |

Note: The bureau originally set the purchase price at one copper coin for every two rice borer moths or eggs. Due to the low number of purchases, on July 22, a notice was issued to all institutes to increase the purchase price to one copper coin for each rice borer egg mass. Subsequently, the price reverted to the original, and on August 25, it was further reduced to one copper coin for every four rice borer moths or eggs.

Advising Against Using US Wheat as Seed 153

The Shanghai County Government received an order yesterday from the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Agriculture and Mines advising against using US wheat borrowed by China as seed. The original order stated, "An agreement has been reached regarding the shipping of US wheat for disaster relief. However, the purchased US wheat should only be used as relief grain for human consumption and should not be used as seed. This is because the source of the US wheat is uncertain, and the vast land and water transportation make it inevitable that there will be stale and rotten seeds, which are not easy to germinate. In addition, the climate and soil of our country are too different from those of the United States. According to the principles of seed transfer and practical experience, it is impossible to adopt it rashly, which would mislead agricultural affairs. We are sincerely afraid that our country's farmers lack scientific knowledge and are in disaster and poverty, so they will not have time to choose carefully and will easily misuse the US wheat as seed. We should take precautions in advance and advise them in advance to avoid mistakes. As for seeds in disaster areas, the Ministry has already ordered local arrangements to be made in order to avoid delaying agricultural time."

Shanghai Epidemic Hospital Extends Closing Date 156

The Shanghai Epidemic Hospital is scheduled to open on July 1st and close on September 30th of the Gregorian calendar each year. This year, since the hospital opened, it has treated 10,000 people, with over 2,000 hospitalized. Daily and nightly treatments are provided, and medical expenses are not charged. Of the 300 cases of true cholera discovered in Shanghai, over 200 were treated at the hospital, accounting for nearly two-thirds. Recently, the hospital, in view of the epidemic situation in Shanghai not abating, convened a board meeting a few days ago and extended the closing date by half a month (until October 15th). Although the hospital has been affected by the current situation and its donation income is not abundant, it has not hesitated due to financial difficulties.
