Paternal Nephew and Son-in-Law Dispute Property 159

Gao Chenghua, a local villager, hired lawyer Xu Yannian to file a lawsuit in the Civil Division of the Second Special District Court, claiming that Gao Yueting, the plaintiff's uncle, only had one daughter, who was married to Chou Shenghua. Gao Yueting had no sons, so he adopted the plaintiff as his heir, as evidenced by a family meeting record. Unexpectedly, after Yueting and his wife passed away one after another, all the inheritance was occupied by Chou Shenghua. Attempts to reason with him were ignored, so the lawsuit was filed, requesting the court to order the defendant to hand over the property in full. The court summoned the parties yesterday based on the complaint. Plaintiff Gao Chenghua first stated the facts. Defendant Chou Shenghua stated that he was in fact taken in as a son-in-law to Gao Yueting's family. As both son-in-law and adopted son, Yueting and his wife did not establish the plaintiff as an heir when they were alive. There is a memorial tablet for Yueting's 20th anniversary stating that the plaintiff is a nephew, which proves this. He requested a clear investigation and hired a lawyer to handle everything on his behalf. The judge dismissed them and adjourned the hearing to a later date.

Marrying a Wife and Encountering a "Dove Release" 160

Xu Naikang, a native of Yancheng from No. 33 Xiaoxin Village, Dacaojia Ferry, Shanghai West, is 36 years old. Due to poverty, he has not yet married. Recently, due to years of savings, he had over 200 yuan and thus thought of seeking a wife. Therefore, he often told his fellow villagers that he was getting old, and of the three unfilial acts, having no descendants is the greatest. Therefore, he wanted to find a wife, but feared that it would be difficult to attract a young woman because of his old age. Fan Tinggui, a neighbor, offered to act as a matchmaker, saying that he had a niece, Zhao Di, who was 23 years old and still a virgin. If he did not mind her being unsophisticated, he was willing to arrange a marriage. Xu asked about the bride price, and Fan discussed it with him. As a result, they agreed on 130 yuan. On the 17th of this month, the bride entered the house and a new-style civilized wedding ceremony was actually held in the shed. A marriage certificate was signed, with Fan Tinggui as the witness. Unexpectedly, after the marriage, the bride was not a virgin. Xu did not mind. However, only ten days after the wedding, on the 28th of this month, the bride suddenly disappeared. Xu was shocked when he returned home. He believed that Fan Tinggui was clearly a "dove release," deceiving him and defrauding him of his money. Therefore, he brought Fan to the Sixth District Police Station, who turned him over to the local court for interrogation.

Page 16

Reader Correspondence

Mr. Someone's Inquiry (Dissatisfied with Wife) 161

I am a young man who has neither brothers nor sisters, and is of marriageable age. Moreover, I am a descendant of both families. Therefore, my parents love me very much. After graduating from junior high school at the age of seventeen, I started to make a living in society. Therefore, my parents were very strict in choosing my marriage partner. As a result, either the girl from this family had a too short life, or the girl from that family had conflicting horoscopes, and none of them were suitable. This is because my family is still an old-fashioned family. It happened that my maternal uncle's eldest daughter was one year younger than me. Relatives had jokingly said when she was young that she would be my wife in the future. When I grew up, my aunt also asked me in person if I agreed. I replied that I was working outside and had achieved nothing, so I dared not talk about this important matter at this time (this was when I was eighteen). That's because I had already rejected it. Unexpectedly, my aunt came forward to bring up the old matter again. My uncle and aunt immediately agreed. However, I had one condition first. Please let her study for two years to gain some common knowledge. If there was a possibility of marriage, then we would get engaged. Unexpectedly, my uncle was also a stubborn person, and he did not agree. Although I strongly opposed it, I couldn't disobey my parents' orders, so I got engaged. I ignored it. The following year, I couldn't bear it any longer and carried out a family revolution. Later, my parents said that they had given birth to eight brothers and sisters, and now there is only you. Now that we are engaged to the daughter of your uncle's family, after she marries into the family, she will definitely be close to her aunt, and there is no reason why they cannot get along well. As parents, we will never do anything wrong. Furthermore, your cousin is also an old-fashioned woman. Now that we are engaged, if she suddenly regrets the marriage, outsiders will suspect that there is another reason, and there may be a matter of life or death. You should think about it. I temporarily took this into consideration and vaguely agreed, seeking to preserve things by compromising. Due to a moment's difference in thought, I have made a lifelong regret, and it is too late to regret it now. I got married last year, but within a month, there were constant conflicts, and there were two big fights, and even a case of swallowing gold to commit suicide. But it is not that I am good at fighting with her, but that her mouth is too garrulous. She asks when she shouldn't ask and doesn't ask when she should ask. I don't want to have meaningless arguments with her, so I ignore her, and she gets angry. After marriage, I have taught her to read novels and practice writing in large and small characters (because she had also read a few days of "Daughter's Classic" from a private tutor when she was young). Unexpectedly, she has never written a single word. I also don't like her behavior. She can't handle household chores either. After I finish work, I go home, sit for a while, and then go out. We have never exchanged three or five words. After the two big fights in the family, my parents also knew that her behavior was wrong and knew that a big mistake had been made and there was no way to undo it. They can only encourage me to work hard and find another wife for me in the future to comfort them. However, I will never do this because of the crime of bigamy, which is not a legitimate practice and is not allowed by current law. So now I simply live like a year, with nothing to look forward to. I only wish that one of us would die, then there would be a bright path to take. But that is not humanitarian. If I talk about divorce, then her uncle will not allow it. Therefore, I am deeply pessimistic. Life is boring and death is impossible. I am in a dilemma. If I cannot take a step back in the future, I will eventually commit suicide to end this miserable life. I am specifically stating the matter clearly to you and hope that you can indicate the most appropriate and fundamental solution, which will save a life and be better than building a seven-story pagoda. But there is absolutely no hope of reconciling, so I hope you can give me advice other than this.

(Reply) Life has its own meaning and important responsibilities. Is it worth it to be so concerned about a mere marriage problem? In ancient times, some people dedicated themselves to the country and did not want to have a family, or even if they had one, they did not want it. You have your own profession, and judging from your letter, you have considerable education. You can seek spiritual comfort and recreation elsewhere. If the family is peaceful, then let it be. Otherwise, let it be. If you can persuade her to change her unsatisfactory words and actions, that would be best. Otherwise, slowly let her realize it herself and implement the method of subtle influence from a psychological perspective. Perhaps as she gets older and her environment changes, she will naturally become aware. If you become pessimistic so quickly and even talk about suicide, you are taking life too lightly and family too seriously, forgetting the kindness of your parents giving birth to you and society raising you, and disregarding your heavenly duty. Only those with knowledge will sneer at you. As for divorce and bigamy, since they are not allowed by law, they will only cause trouble for yourself and increase disputes. You are right not to advocate them.

Affix this stamp when corresponding, along with the appropriate postage stamps.

Robbery on Baker Road to Be Sentenced 163

At around 6 pm on the 14th of this month, the home of Xu Chunhua, an Erren [Shanghai slang for person from Ningbo], at No. 908 Baker Road, was robbed of valuables worth 193 yuan. The Chinese and Western detectives of the Huishan Police Station arrested the perpetrators, Sheng Wanxing, Wang Changyou, Jin A Bao, also known as Gengtang, and Zhang Axing and Li A Ming, Qingkou natives who supplied the firearms, along with suspect Wang Arong, and handed them over to the First Special District Court for interrogation. Yesterday morning, the police sent the six suspects, including Sheng, to the Third Criminal Court for continued trial. According to the police lawyer Zhang Tianyin, the facts of the case were stated, and it was said that during the change of date, it was found that defendant Wang Arong was not related to the case and requested to be released. Then, the victim Xu Chunhua stated that the defendant Sheng Wanxing was indeed present at the scene of the robbery, but he could not identify the others. Sheng Wanxing confessed that he was invited by Zhou Genfu, a bald man on the run, to commit the robbery, and he was also the one who held the gun. Wang Changyou confessed that he was outside as a lookout at the time and did not enter the house. He received 13 yuan afterward. Jin Gengtang Hong and Zhou Genfu knew each other. They gathered and discussed the matter in a Huajie Road teahouse beforehand. The gun was also taken by him. He admitted that he went to commit the robbery. Li A Ming confessed that he knew a person on the run named A Shun, who had a Mauser pistol and asked him to exchange it for a handgun. Therefore, he asked Zhang Axing to find a way. He did not go to the robbery. Zhang Axing confessed that he was a road worker in the Shanghai Municipal Council and knew Li A Ming. The rest of his confession was evasive. Wang Arong confessed that he knew nothing about the robbery and was arrested by mistake. After Judge Shen Bingrong verified the confessions, he instructed the lawyers to make their arguments. He ordered that Wang Arong be released first, and the rest be returned to custody for sentencing at a later date.

Yan Ziyu Discusses Egg Product Registration Rules 164

After the Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau announced the egg product registration rules, Mr. Yan Ziyu, manager of the China Central Cold Storage Plant, told people yesterday that according to the egg product foreign trade registration rules, six reputable companies in the same industry should be obtained as guarantors. However, there are only six ice egg companies in Shanghai. Except for one company that has registered with the government, the other four are purely foreign merchants. Chinese businessmen wanting to ask foreign merchants for a guarantee, the foreign merchants certainly wouldn't agree. Even if they do, it will damage the national dignity. Therefore, the factory has submitted a clear statement to the authorities, adding "but those guaranteed by two reputable non-industry merchants shall also be allowed to register" at the end of Article 2 of the rules, or changed to "the bureau will send personnel to the factory to guide and supervise the packing, and after the packing is completed, the ladder will be sealed, and the key will be kept by the bureau personnel, and it will be opened before export and transported to the warehouse, and the salary of the bureau personnel will be borne by the factory." This advance measure seems to be very appropriate, and it is hoped that the authorities can accommodate it.

Transfer of Public Security Bureau Chiefs 165

Tang Jinghuan, chief of the Third District Second Branch (stationed in Yangjing Town, Pudong) of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, has been transferred by Director Chen to the Second District Second Branch. Zhang Guirong, the current chief of the Second District Second Branch, has been transferred back to serve as chief of the Fifth District Third Branch. Yao Benyuan, the current chief of the Fifth District Third Branch, has been transferred to serve as chief of the Third District Second Branch. They have all taken office.

Zhongbiao Painting Agency Adds Showcase Arrangement Department 166

Since its establishment, the Zhongbiao Painting Agency has been marking its products with a triangular inlaid M-shaped logo for five years. Although the cost of painting on behalf is slightly higher than the public, the products are indeed excellent. They are even more skilled at showcasing locations. Currently, the Shanghai Bank's solicited paintings and the Bank of China's logo won the first prize. The Shanghai Bank's eight-branch showcase is also arranged by the agency. The agency's creations are rich in novel art, and it knows the principles of color and three-dimensional patterns, which can guarantee merchant satisfaction. Contact address: No. 96 Beijing Road, Shanghai, Telephone 15870.

Plum Garden for Sale 167

In Chegouqiao Town, the Second District of Shanghai County, a certain gentleman and merchant Wu invested in the purchase of over 40 mu of farmland in the town and developed it into a plum garden, specializing in planting fine Hangzhou plums, totaling about 1,000 trees. Each year, they produce a large number of fruits, which are purchased by major tea, food, and confectionery shops in Shanghai. Now that the owner has passed away and the family has no intention of operating it, they plan to sell it at a reduced price. Those interested in taking over can contact Mr. Qiao Jiyuan of the Shanghai County Party Headquarters on Fenglai Road, Nanshi, in this city.

Trade Union News 168

The Board of Directors of the China Merchants Bureau's No. 5 Wharf Trade Union held its ninth temporary meeting yesterday. Resolutions: (1) The Nan Zhan Branch Committee submitted a request from the coal yard workers to join the association. The meeting decided to hand it over to the organization department for review and handling. (2) To organize a national anti-Japanese salvation committee, Xue Yinkui, Ye Yufu, Li Angqing, Jiang Juncui, Shen Zhichen, Jin Jixiang, Chen Shijun, Zhang Guiqing, Yu Xianting, Bian Changru, Liang Jilin, Hu Maolin, Li Chunrong, Wang Jielu, Shi Zhang, Shan Xishou, Shen Xiaru, Xia Yinxu, Cheng Changsheng, Lu Jianian, Wu Jucai, Zhu Lansheng, and Chen Bonian were appointed as members. The resolution was passed.

The Binding Industry Union held a city-wide representative conference on the 25th. The presidium consisted of Lu Jianqiu, Chen Zhaonong, and Ren Changfu. The ceremony was performed as usual. The presidium reported on the atrocities of the Japanese army. After the report, a unanimous resolution was passed: (1) This association and association are willing to lead all workers to organize a volunteer army and act as the vanguard of all sectors of the country. (2) Organize a propaganda team to give lectures and expose the truth about the Japanese invasion of China. (3) (Omitted) (4) Regarding union affairs: (1) The resignations of Zhao Jialing, Ge Guangrong, Chen Shaosong, Jiang Shangzhen, and Xu Fuli, who had repeatedly resigned, were resolved. The resignations of Ge Guangrong and Chen Shaosong were not approved. The resignations of the other three comrades were approved. (2) Feng Shaoquan and Huang Songyue really cannot come to the meeting to work. The meeting decided to allow them to be relieved of their duties. (3) Zhang Haosheng and Chao Guosheng have been absent from meetings many times and have neglected union affairs. The meeting decided to send a letter in the name of the representative conference to urge them to come to the meeting to work immediately. (4) How to fill the vacancies in the council and supervisors was resolved by electing Lu Jianqiu, Xue Lanxin, Shen Changjiang, Xia Songfu, and He Shengae separately (5) The association is facing economic difficulties. The meeting decided to appoint Xue Lanxin, Shen Changjiang, Lu Jianqiu, Sun Zhaolu, He Shengae, and Qian Fubao to be responsible for collecting donations to eliminate abuses. (6) Most of the Western clothing stores are in charge, violating the treaty, and even deducting 10% of wages. It was resolved to present it to the higher level and order the capital to fulfill the contract. If they violate it again, report to the Public Security Bureau for accusation and punishment. After the resolutions were passed, the meeting adjourned at 10:30.

The Sixth District Tea Industry Union held its tenth board meeting yesterday. Chairman Wu Bochao opened the meeting as usual. The chairman reported that in addition to the union's affairs, there was also a major matter to report, that is, the heavy flood this year, especially in Sangzi (Anhui). The union has launched a fundraising campaign for the flood relief, and more than 700 yuan has been raised. Should the union donate all the money to Sangzi, or how should it be allocated for flood relief, let everyone decide. Discussion: (1) Shen Tai Tea Warehouse sent a letter the day before yesterday stating that its business had failed and declared bankruptcy. The meeting decided that in order to understand the truth, Cheng Ganting and Hu Chenglin should be sent to investigate and verify the facts before making a decision. (2) Should the working hours of the union workers be changed? The meeting decided to hand it over to the next board meeting for decision. (3) How much money should be donated for this fundraising for flood relief? The meeting decided to send 240 yuan to the flood relief societies in the provinces, and the rest to the Anhui Flood Relief Association in Shanghai. The resolution was passed. (4) The union has always had a festival fee of 8 yuan to subsidize each staff member during the Mid-Autumn Festival. This year, due to the heavy flood, should all the money be donated for flood relief? The meeting decided to pass it. (5) In addition to donating the festival fee, should the union staff make another donation? The meeting decided that everyone would donate voluntarily. As a result, Wu Bochao donated 10 yuan, Cheng Ganting, Hu Chenglin, Hong Xinyuan, and He Yuren each donated 5 yuan, and Wang Zuyin donated 2 yuan. (6) The union will donate another 30 yuan due to the heavy flood in Anhui. The resolution was passed. (7) The meeting ended after the discussion.

Weather Report 170

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated: Cloudy and cold weather in the Yangtze River basin and coastal areas; strong northerly winds over the Yellow Sea and East China Sea. Also, within the 24 hours before 3:00 PM yesterday, the highest temperature in this city was 67.1, and the lowest was 56.1. On the same day last year, the highest was 76.6, and the lowest was 66.2.

Shanghai Market

Commercial News 171

The ladies' department of Taixing Company, No. 23 Nanjing Road, announces that a large batch of autumn fabrics has newly arrived at the company, with hundreds of varieties of colors and patterns. Cheongsams, flannels for coats, and French floral silks are very popular among women, and there is a tendency for demand to exceed supply. Ladies from all walks of life who wish to choose new autumn fabrics should not miss this opportunity, etc.

Bee Brand woolen yarn is manufactured by a famous British factory, with soft and durable quality, and has been sold in China for a long time with an outstanding reputation, which is well-known to women and children. Recently, due to the expanding scope of business, there are more and more counterfeiters. Now, in order to maintain its reputation and prevent customers from being deceived, the manufacturer of this product has changed the trademark of its four types of woolen yarns, including Four-Strand Beehive, Six Bees, Scholar, and Giant, to a blue background with white patterns hard-printed inside each skein, starting from June of this year, for identification and to prevent the sale of counterfeit goods, etc.

American Victor Talking Machine Company announces that, in view of the Chinese people's love of music, the company has established a factory in Shanghai to manufacture records. The factory site is located at the corner of Pingliang Road and Ningwu Road in Eastern Shanghai. The groundbreaking ceremony was held yesterday afternoon. In addition to all Chinese and foreign employees of the company, there were also Chinese and foreign guests, and managers from various Victor agencies. Mr. Kunod, the US Commercial Counselor, performed the groundbreaking ceremony and delivered a congratulatory speech. Mr. Qiu Liang, the manager of the company, entertained the guests with tea and refreshments, and then they dispersed. This factory will be able to start production in three months, with construction costs of one million, etc.

Medical News 172

Dr. Zhao Nanshi, a specialist in mental illness from Zhujiaqiao, Nanhui, Pudong, announces that the ancestral natural manic grass has great efficacy and has long been famous at home and abroad. Since the establishment of the Shanghai General Distribution Office in Maoye Lane, Wangjia Wharf, South Shanghai, sales have been booming. However, unscrupulous merchants take the opportunity to counterfeit, and counterfeit medicines have been found on the market. Now, resolute rectification is being carried out. Shanghai employees are secretly visiting and investigating those who are counterfeiting. On the other hand, special commissioners have been sent to Nanjing to find a suitable location to establish a Nanjing branch distribution office to benefit patients and prevent counterfeiting. Mr. Qu Yueyang and Mr. Mo, two major lawyers, have now been hired as legal advisors, etc.
